# country
on_religion_change = {
	on_religion_change_effect = yes
	on_religion_change_estate_privileges_effect = yes
	#judaism_on_religion_change_effect = yes

	set_country_flag = changed_religion #general-purpose

	if = { #Save the EoA if the emperor is force converted
		limit = {
			is_emperor = yes
			NOT = {
				religion_group = cannorian 
				hre_reform_passed = anbennar_imperial_dynasty # this is here for unlikely candidate achievement
			}
		}
		set_emperor = no
	}

	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { religion = night_coven }
			NOT = { religion = shadow_pact }
			tag = S70
		}
		#remove night coven Reforms if you convert away
		remove_country_modifier = night_coven_reform_1_m
	}

	#removes corinite holy order upgrade modifiers
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = upgraded_balgar
			NOT = { religion = corinite }	#this only needs to check when you convert away from Corinite
		}
		every_owned_province = { remove_province_modifier = corinite_balgar_upgraded }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = upgraded_corin
			NOT = { religion = corinite }	#this only needs to check when you convert away from Corinite
		}
		every_owned_province = { remove_province_modifier = corinite_corin_upgraded }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = upgraded_falah
			NOT = { religion = corinite }	#this only needs to check when you convert away from Corinite
		}
		every_owned_province = { remove_province_modifier = corinite_falah_upgraded }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = upgraded_munas
			NOT = { religion = corinite }	#this only needs to check when you convert away from Corinite
		}
		every_owned_province = { remove_province_modifier = corinite_munas_upgraded }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = upgraded_ryala
			NOT = { religion = corinite }	#this only needs to check when you convert away from Corinite
		}
		every_owned_province = { remove_province_modifier = corinite_ryala_upgraded }
	}

	#removes ravelian modifiers
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Emperor" } }
		remove_country_modifier = first_council_harsh
		remove_country_modifier = first_council_conciliatory
		remove_country_modifier = second_council_harsh
		remove_country_modifier = second_council_conciliatory
		remove_country_modifier = third_council_harsh
		remove_country_modifier = third_council_conciliatory
		remove_country_modifier = fourth_council_harsh
		remove_country_modifier = fourth_council_conciliatory
		if = {
			limit = { religion = ravelian }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = first_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = first_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = first_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = first_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = second_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = second_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = second_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = second_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = third_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = third_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = third_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = third_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = fourth_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = fourth_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = fourth_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = fourth_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#move aakhet if the host converts
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_country_flag = current_aakhet_host 
			NOT = { religion = aakhetist }
		}
		aakhet_movement = yes
	}
	#reset approval if you convert away
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { religion = aakhetist } check_variable = { aakhet_approval = 1 } }
		set_variable = { aakhet_approval = 0 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = corinite
		}
		set_country_flag = converted_to_corinite
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = ravelian
		}
		set_country_flag = converted_to_ravelian
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = god_fragment_chamber } 
			province_event = { id = ravelian.25 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = suhans_praxis
		}
		set_country_flag = converted_to_suhans_praxis
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = bav_religious_mandate_mod }
		remove_country_modifier = bav_religious_mandate_mod
	}
	add_country_modifier = {
		name = recently_changed_religion_dummy
		duration = 10
		hidden = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = { religion = mother_akasik }
		#Mother Akasik mountain count up on conversion
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 383 }
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 390 }
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 392 }
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 395 }
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 396 }
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 397 }
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 398 }
		mother_akasik_province = { gained = yes prov = 401 }
	}
	else = {
		#Mother Akasik mountain count down on conversion
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 383 }
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 390 }
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 392 }
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 395 }
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 396 }
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 397 }
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 398 }
		mother_akasik_province = { lost = yes prov = 401 }
	}

	#Mother Akasik normal conversion
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = mother_akasik
			NOT = { owns = 383 }
			NOT = { owns = 390 }
			NOT = { owns = 392 }
			NOT = { owns = 395 }
			NOT = { owns = 396 }
			NOT = { owns = 397 }
			NOT = { owns = 398 }
			NOT = { owns = 401 }
		}
		country_event = { id = mother_akasik.3 }
	}

	#Converting into Ynnic religion
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				religion = ynn_river_worship
				religion = ynn_river_reformed
			}
		}
		ynnic_setup_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = ynn_river_worship_flag }
			}
			set_country_flag = stuir_balia_visible	#Get Stuir Balia notification upon converting to YRW
		}
		set_country_flag = ynn_river_worship_flag	#add a tracker for cleanup when converting out
		country_event = { id = ynn_zodiac.3 }	#Ynn Worship deity set

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_regency = no
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_1
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_2
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_3
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_4
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_5
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_6
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_7
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_8
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_9
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_10
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_11
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_12
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_13
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_14
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_15
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_ruler_16
				}
			}
			ruler_ynn_zodiac = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_regency = yes
				NOT = {
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_1
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_2
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_3
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_4
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_5
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_6
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_7
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_8
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_9
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_10
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_11
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_12
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_13
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_14
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_15
					has_ruler_modifier = ynn_zodiac_heir_16
				}
			}
			heir_ynn_zodiac = yes
		}

		cannorian_in_ynn_rename = yes
	}
	#Reforming OR converting out of Ynn River Worship
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ynn_river_worship_flag
			NOT = {
				religion = ynn_river_worship
			}

# country. Spawned when Enforcing Rebel Demands through a Support Rebels-war.
on_enforce_rebel_demands = {
	# ROOT = The winning country
	# FROM = The loosing country
	set_country_flag = helped_rebels_win_war

	events = {
		flavour_brelar.13		# Boats revolt
		flavour_beggaston.2		# Freodam invasion
	}

	#Fangaulan Pantheon
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = fangaulan_pantheon
		}
		add_church_power = 30
	}
}

# country
on_colonial_liberation = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = old_world_to_new_world_flag }
			#Anbennar: Urdea Samrad isn't supposed to change government upon independence
			NOT = { tag = U42 }
		}
		country_event = { id = colonial_nation.90 days = 1 }
	}
	#Anbennar: Urdea Samrad should get their proper color upon independence
	else_if = {
		limit = { tag = U42 }
		country_event = { id = flavor_urdea_samrad.2 days = 1 }
	}
}

# country
on_colonial_reintegration = {
	events = {
		colonial_nation.91
	}
}

# country
on_peace_actor = {
	events = {
		# usa_dlc.36			# Evacuation Day
		deepwoods.12			# Give wood elf territory back
		flavor_krakazol.42		#krakazol ale war
		effelai_worship.536		# laii humilation of taychend
		gushuokguan_event.38	#Gushuokguan Civil War
		gushuokguan_event.39	#Gushuokguan Civil War
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_at_war = no
			has_country_modifier = blorc_ruler_shows_prowess
		}
		remove_country_modifier = blorc_ruler_shows_prowess
	}
	if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = deepwoods_verdant_pact }
		country_event = { id = deepwoods.1 days = 45 random = 45 } # End the Verdant Pact, if Wood Elves collectively have enough provinces.
	}
	#Tribal Chendhyans
	if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = {
				has_reform = chendhyan_tribal_federation 
				has_reform = chendhyan_federation_to_ezhudar
			}
		}
		every_neighbor_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			reverse_add_casus_belli = {
				type = cb_tribal_raiding
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	every_neighbor_country = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_reform = chendhyan_tribal_federation 
				has_reform = chendhyan_federation_to_ezhudar
			}
			NOT = { overlord_of = ROOT }
		}
		add_casus_belli = {
			type = cb_tribal_raiding
			target = ROOT
		}
	}
	if = { # Harpylen. Do this when you win or lose a war
		limit = {
			tag = F98
			mission_completed = F98_spreading_wings
		}
		FROM = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = F98_spreading_our_wings
			}
		}
	}
}

	events = {
		flavor_krakazol.42		#krakazol ale war

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_at_war = no
			has_country_modifier = blorc_ruler_shows_prowess
		}
		remove_country_modifier = blorc_ruler_shows_prowess
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = verne_union_target is_subject_of = A33 }
		change_religion = corinite
		change_government_to_monarchy = yes
		clr_country_flag = verne_union_target
	}

	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = vt_outmatched }
		remove_country_modifier = vt_outmatched
	}
	if = { # Harpylen. Do this when you win or lose a war
		limit = {
			tag = F98
			mission_completed = F98_spreading_wings
		}
		FROM = {
			every_owned_province = {
				remove_province_modifier = F98_spreading_our_wings
			}
		}
	}
}

# country
# root = winning country, from = loser country
on_war_won = {
	#FROM = { country_event = { id = flavor_cri.6 } }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = can_gain_legendary_pirates_flag
			NOT = { has_ruler_flag = historical_pirate }
			has_government_attribute = is_pirate_republic_reform
			FROM = { total_development = ROOT }
		}
		# random = { #Anbennar: commented cause we don't have the event
			# chance = 5
			# country_event = {
				# id = pirates.25
			# }
		# }
	}
	ROOT = { country_event = { id = tributary_events.32 } }
	# ROOT = { country_event = { id = xhazobkult_events.1 } } #Xhazobkult tributaries
	ROOT = { country_event = { id = anb_miscevents.21 } } #Removing corinite buff during league war
	ROOT = { country_event = { id = flavour_plumstead.28 } }

	if = {	#for pdx num_of_wars scripted trigger need to set the country_flag first
		limit = { has_country_flag = count_wars_won }
		change_variable = {
			which = num_of_wars_won_var
			value = 1
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = leader_illegitimate
					has_country_flag = leader_legitimate
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = leader_illegitimate
					has_country_flag = leader_legitimate
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = { country_event = { id = goldisland.13 } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			mission_completed = B28_i_have_an_announcement_to_make
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = B28_not_shown_off
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = B28_mockery
					}
				}
				humiliated_by = ROOT
			}
			add_treasury = -100
			ROOT = {
				add_mil_power = 50
				add_dip_power = 50
				add_adm_power = 50
				add_war_exhaustion = -5
				if = {
						limit = { NOT = { stability = -2 } }
						add_stability = 1
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = orc_clans_contribution
					duration = 3650
				}
				add_treasury = 100
			}
			remove_opinion = {
					WHO = ROOT
					modifier = B28_mockery
			}
			reverse_remove_opinion = {
				WHO = ROOT 
				modifier = B28_mockery
			}
			clr_country_flag = B28_not_shown_off
		}
	}
	if = {

		change_variable = { nbWarWon = 1 }
	}

	if = {	#temple plunder reparations

			has_country_flag = temple_plundered_tag@ROOT
		}
		country_event = {
			id = spirits.422
			days = 5
		}
	}
	FROM = {

			limit = {
				has_country_flag = temple_plundered_tag@THIS
			}

				id = spirits.422
				days = 5

	}

	if = {

			is_emperor = yes
			has_subject_of_type = imperial_bodyguard

			tag = A77
		}

				which = orda_conversion_war
				value =  1

	if = {

			has_saved_global_event_target = salt_and_silence_giant

		if = {

				}
			}
		}

		country_event = {
			id = yemotaferi.6
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = ardimya_war_of_independence
			FROM = { has_country_flag = ardimya_war_of_independence_colonial_power }
		}
		clr_country_flag = ardimya_war_of_independence
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = ardimya_war_of_independence_colonial_power }
		country_event = {
			id = ardimya.8
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ardimya.9
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = track_wars_won_against_primary_enemy_of_different_religion
			FROM = { NOT = { has_matching_religion = ROOT } }
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = religiousVictories
			value = 1
		}
	}

	S45_victory_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = mechanim_self_reflection }
		add_church_power = 50
	}
}

		every_country = {
			remove_country_modifier = A90_bardic_influence_1
			remove_country_modifier = A90_bardic_influence_2
			remove_country_modifier = A90_bardic_influence_3
			remove_country_modifier = A90_bardic_influence_4
			remove_country_modifier = A90_bardic_influence_5
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { is_subject_of_type = acolyte_dominion }
		subtract_variable = { aInfluence = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { aInfluence = 0 } } }
			set_variable = { aInfluence = 0 }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = Z99
			has_country_flag = black_overseer_invasion
			any_known_country = {
				if = {
					limit = { war_with = Z99 }
					NOT = {
						any_owned_province = {
							OR = {
								region = kheterata_region
								region = akasik_region
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = black_overseer_invasion
		remove_country_modifier = black_overseer_1
		remove_country_modifier = black_overseer_2
		remove_country_modifier = black_overseer_3
		remove_country_modifier = black_overseer_4
		remove_country_modifier = black_overseer_5
		remove_country_modifier = black_overseer_6
	}

	if = {    #Clears alliances for Ynnic Overlord
        limit = {
            FROM = {                             # if the winner has,
                ynnic_iosahar = 1                    # 1+ ynnic iosahar,
                has_country_modifier = ynn_diplo    # ynn_diplo mod,
                num_of_allies = 1                    # 1+ allies,
            }                                    # then do:
        }
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				capital_scope = { superregion = ynn_superregion } 
				alliance_with = ROOT
			}
			ROOT = {
				break_alliance = PREV
			}
		}
        #ROOT = {
			#if = {
                #limit = {                            # if loser is iosahar of winner,
                    #is_subject_of = FROM
                    #is_subject_of_type = ynnic_iosahar
                #}                                    # then do:
				#create_subject = {                        # turn winner into vassal of loser (switcheroo)
					#subject_type = vassal
					#subject = FROM
				#}
				#FROM = {
					#grant_independence = yes            # turn winner independent again
					#create_subject = {                    # turn loser into iosahar of winner
						#subject_type = ynnic_iosahar
						#subject = ROOT
					#}
				#}
			#}
        #}
    }
	
	if = { #sanity check for Command suddenly surrendering
		limit = { 
			has_country_flag = command_leadership_flag_@FROM
		}
		clr_country_flag = command_leadership_flag_@FROM
	}

	if = { #Bulwar incident end
		limit = {
			tag = F39
			FROM = { tag = F28 }
		}
		country_event = { id = flavour_bulwar_tag.15 }
	}

	#triggered modifiers replacements
	remove_country_modifier = anb_defense_of_empire

	#Drozma Tur
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = drozma_tur
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dt_war_leader_against@ROOT
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = dt_war_leader_against@ROOT
			every_known_country = {
				clr_country_flag = dt_ally_to_leader_against@ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = drozma_tur
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = dt_ally_to_leader_against@ROOT
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = dt_ally_to_leader_against@ROOT
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = dt_war_leader_against@ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { owns = 4630 }
		4630 = { add_great_project_tier = { type = iron_palace tier = -1 } }
	}

	if = { #istralore corinite flipping
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					FROM = {
						has_country_flag = A45_victory_on_halann_flag
					}
					is_part_of_hre = yes
				}
				AND = {
					FROM = {
						has_country_flag = A45_spear_and_shield
					}
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							continent = africa
							continent = europe
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = istralore.26
		}
	}
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = molten_eternity
			has_personal_deity = volcanic_truth_zeal
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moltenEternityObligationVar
			value = -50
		}
	}
	clr_country_flag = I78_released_provinces
	
	update_artifice_points = yes #needs to be last
}

	#Taychend Glory
	if = {

			has_country_flag = taychendi_coalition_defender
		}
		clr_country_flag = taychendi_coalition_defender
	}

	if = { #Nekheis and their overlord lose their war modifiers
		limit = { has_country_modifier = nekhei_granted_war_rights }
		remove_country_modifier = nekhei_granted_war_rights
		overlord = {
			remove_all_nekhei_negate_overlord_modifiers = yes
		}
	}
	
	if = { #Besolaki
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = G54_in_okti_arped_war_flag
		}
		clr_country_flag = G54_in_okti_arped_war_flag
		set_country_flag = G54_oktikheion_war_happened_flag
		country_event = {
			id = besolaki_events.16
		}
	}

	#Sri Baginda
	if = {
		limit = { is_sri_baginda = yes }
		add_sri_baginda_power = { value = -25 }
	}
}

# country
# root = loser country, from = winner country
on_battle_lost_country = {
	on_battle_lost_country_effect = yes
	on_battle_ended_effect = yes

	random_events = {
		90 = 0
		10 = friendship_events.1 #Historical Friendship Broken
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = desert_legion_mechanic
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = JaddariDeathCount
			value = 0
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = JaddariDeathCount
			which = land_units_killed 
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = JaddariDeathCount
			which = land_units_lost 
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = JaddariDeathCount
					value = 1000
				}
			}
			add_government_power = { mechanic_type = desert_legion_mechanic power_type = jaddari_zealotry value = 1 }
			subtract_variable = {
				which = JaddariDeathCount
				value = 1000
			}
		}
	}

	#Venomtooth unit killed count
	if = {
		limit = { tag = B22 }
		change_variable = {
			which = vt_units_killed
			which = land_units_lost
		}
	}

	dragon_turtles_casualty_friendship_effect = yes
}

# province
# root = location, from = loser country
on_battle_won_province = {
	on_battle_won_province_effect = yes
	
	# Sacrificing Rebels
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				tag = REB
			}
			owner = {
				religion = xhazobkult
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = xhazobkult_sacrificed_rebels
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = xhazobkult_showed_lenience
				}
			}
			units_in_province = owner # This is a bit of a hack
		}

		random_list = {
			10 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5 # Make it 15% chance for more demonic schools

					owner = { is_demonic_school = yes }
				}

				province_event = {
					id = xhazobkult_events.110
					days = 1
				}
			}
			90 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.94 # Make it 15% chance for more demonic schools

					owner = { is_demonic_school = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	S45_battle_effect = yes

	random_events = {
		900 = 0

		33 = aw_ghouls.110
		67 = aw_ghouls.111	#more common one for spookier places
	}
}

# country
# root = winning country, from = loser country
on_battle_won_country = {
	on_battle_won_country_effect = yes #1.35
	on_battle_ended_effect = yes

	random_events = {
		1000 = 0

		100 = aw_zombies.100
	}

	#averibilet battles agianst trolls won
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = S53_battles_won_against_trolls
			FROM = { tag = S70 }
		}
		S53_won_battle_against_trolls = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = anb_track_casualties_from_battles_won
				has_mission = vanrahar_4_trials_of_strength #generic mission
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = casualties_from_battles_won
			which = land_units_killed
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = casualties_from_battles_won
			which = land_units_lost
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					primary_culture = primal_harimari
					tag = R77
				}
				FROM = { capital_scope = { superregion = bulwar_superregion } }
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = casualties_from_battles_won_bulwar
				which = land_units_killed
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = casualties_from_battles_won_bulwar
				which = land_units_lost
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Accretive Path Chi Stacking
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = accretive_path
			OR = {
				has_church_aspect = accretive_path_universal_martial_education_unimproved
				has_church_aspect = accretive_path_universal_martial_education_improved
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = land_unit_casualties_ap_var
			which = land_units_killed
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = land_unit_casualties_ap_var
			which = land_units_lost
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = land_unit_casualties_ap_var
					value = 1000
				}
			}
			change_variable = { land_unit_casualties_ap_var = -1000 }
			add_church_power = 1
			change_variable = { accretive_path_mil_chi = 1 }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = desert_legion_mechanic
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = JaddariDeathCount
			value = 0
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = JaddariDeathCount
			which = land_units_killed 
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = JaddariDeathCount
			which = land_units_lost 
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = JaddariDeathCount
					value = 1000
				}
			}
			add_government_power = { mechanic_type = desert_legion_mechanic power_type = jaddari_zealotry value = 1 }
			subtract_variable = {
				which = JaddariDeathCount
				value = 1000
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = taychend_vainglory_mechanic
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = TaychendDeathCount
			value = 0
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = TaychendDeathCount
			which = land_units_killed 
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = TaychendDeathCount
			which = land_units_lost 
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = TaychendDeathCount
					value = 1000
				}
			}
			add_government_power = { mechanic_type = taychend_vainglory_mechanic power_type = taychend_vainglory_power value = 0.2 }
			subtract_variable = {
				which = TaychendDeathCount
				value = 1000
			}
		}
	}

	if = { #Golden Tremor
		limit = { 
			has_country_modifier = I57_the_drums_of_reformation 
			FROM = { 
				NOT = { 
					tag = REB
					tag = NAT
				} 
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = GoldenTremorDeathCount
			value = 0
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = GoldenTremorDeathCount
			which = land_units_killed 
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = GoldenTremorDeathCount
					value = 2000
				}
			}
			change_government_reform_progress = 1
			subtract_variable = {
				which = GoldenTremorDeathCount
				value = 2000
			}
		}
	}

	#Raithtall MT check
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { tag = H12 }
			FROM = { religion = winter_court }
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = raithtall_winter_battle_won
			value = 1
		}
	}
	#Dogeater checks
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = dush_dogeater }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_reform = B28_rule_of_the_strong
				}
				FROM = {
					tag = REB
				}
			}
			add_mil_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_adm_power = 10
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = B28_men_flag
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_province_modifier = recent_uprising
					}
					remove_province_modifier = recent_uprising
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = B28_recent_uprising
						duration = 3650
					}
					owner = {
						add_manpower = 1
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = B28_punched_into_submission
							duration = 3650
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = { 
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = B28 } 
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = B27 } 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { religion = regent_court }
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = battle_won_rc
				value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { culture = green_orc }
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = battle_won_go
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Drozma Tur Battle won check
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = drozma_tur
			has_church_aspect = aspire_power_aspect_mil
		}
		add_church_power = 2
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = drozma_tur
			has_church_aspect = aspire_power_aspect_adm
			FROM = {
				tag = REB
			}
		}
		add_church_power = 5
	}

	#Frozenmaw Moskaran Conscription
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = moskaran_conscription_0
				has_country_modifier = moskaran_conscription_1
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moskaranCasualties
			which = land_units_lost
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #upgrade from lv0 to lv1 at 10000
				has_country_modifier = moskaran_conscription_0
				check_variable = { which = moskaranCasualties value = 10000 }
			}
			country_event = { id = flavor_frozenmaw.41 }
			remove_country_modifier = moskaran_conscription_0 
			clr_country_flag = moskaran_flag_0
			add_country_modifier = { name = moskaran_conscription_1 duration = -1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { #upgrade from lv1 to lv2 at 40000
				has_country_modifier = moskaran_conscription_1
				check_variable = {
					which = moskaranCasualties
					value = 40000 
				}
			} 
			country_event = { id = flavor_frozenmaw.42 }
			remove_country_modifier = moskaran_conscription_1
			add_country_modifier = { name = moskaran_conscription_2 duration = -1 }
		}
	}

	if = { #Magic Rework
		limit = { has_country_modifier = orb_of_omniscience_kill_tracker }
		change_variable = { which = orb_of_omniscience_progress_tracker which = land_units_killed }
		change_variable = { which = orb_of_omniscience_progress_tracker which = land_units_lost }
	}

	#Venomtooth unit killed count
	if = {
		limit = { tag = B22 }
		change_variable = {
			which = vt_units_killed
			which = land_units_killed
		}
	}

	#Wild Hunt Second Great Incursion event
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = I78
			FROM = { culture_group = triunic }
			has_global_flag = I78_caehns_authority_double_no_war
		}
		country_event = { id = flavour_wild_hunt.6 }
	}

	# Yemotaferi Troll Kill Counter
	if = {
		limit = { 
			tag = S50
			FROM = { has_country_modifier = troll_military }
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = S50_troll_battles_won
			value = 1
		}
	}

	#Tsukqiao
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_reform = tsukqiao_throne_of_lies_reform
			NOT = { FROM = { tag = REB } } 
		}
		add_legitimacy = 2
	}

	# Flying Hound
	if = {
		limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = B43 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = B43_stop_counting_battles_won }
				any_ally = {
					OR = {
						is_in_war = { attacker_leader = ROOT }
						is_in_war = { defender_leader = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = B43_battle_won_1 } } set_country_flag = B43_battle_won_1 }
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = B43_battle_won_2 } } set_country_flag = B43_battle_won_2 }
			else = { 
				set_country_flag = B43_stop_counting_battles_won 
				clr_country_flag = B43_battle_won_1
				clr_country_flag = B43_battle_won_2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_ruler_modifier = B43_the_grasshopper_knights
				check_variable = {
					which = land_units_killed
					value = 5000
				}
			}
			change_government_reform_progress = 10
		}
	}

	if = { #Gasha
		limit = { has_country_modifier = L76_shock_and_awe NOT = { has_country_flag = L76_rip_and_tear_mana_refund } }
		change_variable = { which = ripAndTearBattlesWon value = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = ripAndTearBattlesWon value = 10 } }
			change_mana = { amount = 25 }
			set_country_flag = L76_rip_and_tear_mana_refund
		}
	}
	
	dragon_turtles_casualty_friendship_effect = yes
}

	on_battle_lost_unit_effect = yes #1.35

# province
# root = location, from = country doing it
on_added_to_trade_company = {
	if = { #1.35
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_country_flag = adding_provinces_to_trade_c_merc_prod_flag } 
		}
		owner = { add_mercantilism = 1 } 
		add_base_production = 1 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = verne_trade_company_conversion }
			OR = {
				owner = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = A33 } }
				region = akasik_region
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = verne_trade_company_conversion_modifier
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	# Beikdugang
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government_attribute = is_beikdugang_plutocracy
			}
			Y15_calculate_gov_mechanic_ship_trade_power_buff = yes
		}
	}
}

# province
# root = location, from = country doing it
on_removed_from_company = {
	if = { #1.35
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_country_flag = adding_provinces_to_trade_c_merc_prod_flag } 
		}
		owner = { add_mercantilism = -1 } 
		add_base_production = -1 
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_province_modifier = verne_trade_company_conversion_modifier}
		remove_province_modifier = verne_trade_company_conversion_modifier
	}
	# Beikdugang
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government_attribute = is_beikdugang_plutocracy
			}
			Y15_calculate_gov_mechanic_ship_trade_power_buff = yes
		}
	}
}

# province
# root = location, from = winner country
on_battle_lost_province = {
	on_battle_lost_province_effect = yes
	
	###############################################################
	# EFFECTS BELOW HERE DO NOT WORK PROPERLY IN SCRIPTED EFFECTS #
	# most common causes are:                                     #
	# using a country event or similar in an else_if              #
	# or using a trigger switch                                   #
	###############################################################
	
	#karassk merc company wins
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = L68_track_merc_wins
				any_hired_mercenary_company = {
					location = { province_id = ROOT } 
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			change_variable = {
				which = L68_battles_with_merc_won
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	#karassk naval wins 
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = L68_track_naval_wins
			}
			is_sea = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			change_variable = {
				which = L68_battles_with_naval_won
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = drozma_last_stand_prov_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				from = {
					tag = REB
				}
				owner = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ai = no
							has_country_flag = drozma_fighting_last_stand
						}
						overlord = {
							ai = no
							has_country_flag = drozma_fighting_last_stand
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { country_event = { id = ynn_events.27 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				from = {
					tag = REB
				}
				owner = {
					OR = {
						ai = yes
						has_country_flag = drozma_fighting_last_stand
						overlord = {
							ai = yes
							has_country_flag = drozma_fighting_last_stand
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							has_country_flag = drozma_ai_loss_1
						}
					}
				}
				owner = { 
					set_country_flag = drozma_ai_loss_1
				}
			}
			else = {
				owner = { country_event = { id = ynn_events.27 } }
			}
		}
	}	
}

# country
# root = losing country, from = location
on_siege_lost_country = {
	events = {
		curia.8			#curia loses its money, not sure we need new ver
		# papacy_events.5	#AnbennarNewVer
		flavour_tluukt.60
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_subject_of_type = acolyte_dominion }
		subtract_variable = { aInfluence = 0.25 }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { aInfluence = 0 } } }
			set_variable = { aInfluence = 0 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = R62 }
		command_siege_lost_effect = yes
	}

	#Drozma Tur rebel siege check
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = REB 
			FROM = {
				owner = {
					religion = drozma_tur
					has_church_aspect = aspire_power_aspect_mil
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			owner = {
				add_church_power = 5
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_nobles
					loyalty = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Wild Hunt Ultakal owner capital siege
	if = {
		limit = {
			culture_group = triunic
			owns = 5239
			FROM = { is_capital = yes owner = { tag = ROOT } }
			has_global_flag = I78_caehns_authority_double_no_war
		}
		I78 = { country_event = { id = flavour_wild_hunt.7 } }
	}

	#Gushuokguan Siege Counter
	# It's here instead of on_siege_won_country because any_war_enemy_country exists but
	# something like any_war_ally_country does not
	# This logic is because you can form another country, like Yanshen, and keep your MT
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = merc_flying_pebbles_available # Just so we don't need to iterate through several countries for most of the game
			any_war_enemy_country = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = Y17 } #Gushuokguan
				any_hired_mercenary_company = {
					template = merc_flying_pebbles
					location = { province_id = FROM }
				}
			}
		}
		random_war_enemy_country = { # This will only ever be 1 tag
			limit = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = Y17 } #Gushuokguan
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = gushuokguan_siege_counter
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

	#Dragon Turtle
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag_allowed_dragon_turtle_system = yes
			FROM = { fort_level = 1 }
		}
		dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = monzaketzya amount = -4 }
		dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = moiokalakupua amount = -4 }
		dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = hokieal amount = -4 }
		dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = iehu amount = -4 }
	}
}

# province
# root = location, from = losing country
on_siege_won_province = {
	events = {
		flavor_vazhatun.111
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			from = {
				tag = REB
				is_rebel_type = revolutionary_rebels
			}
			owner = {
				any_owned_province = {
					region = root
					has_revolution_in_province = yes
				}
				# NOT = { has_disaster = french_revolution }
				NOT = { has_disaster = revolution }
				NOT = { has_spawned_rebels = revolutionary_rebels }
			}
		}
		owner = { country_event = { id = center_of_revolution.1600 } }
	}
	# Anbennar
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_disaster = magnate_uprising } }
		magnate_uprising_siege_won_effects = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			province_id = 441
			441 = {
				sieged_by = A77
			}
			A77 = { has_country_flag = second_aldresian_crusade }
		}

# province
# root = location, from = winning country
on_siege_lost_province =  {
	events = {
		diggy.13
		magic_project_lichdom.15
		vampire_ruler.100
		spirits.002 #Hidden event to determine if temple is damaged by siege
		allclan.9999 #cede provinces in kinstrife - in province event option to avoid crashing the game
		flavour_zokka.9999 #see above, but for zokka!
		xhazobkult_events.201
	}
	
	if = { # Kobold Traps! (Comes before the rest for siege magic reasons)
		limit = { 
			ROOT = {
				has_province_flag = has_kobold_traps 
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = enchantment_3_dominate_to_surrender_siege_mod }
			} 
			FROM = { NOT = { culture_group = kobold } }
		}
		province_event = { id = kobold_traps.6 } 
	}

	remove_harmful_siege_magic = yes
	# Above effect must happen after all checks for dominate to surrender (enchantment_3_dominate_to_surrender_siege_mod)
	# Checks currently in diggy.13, spirits.002, and kobold_traps.6

	if = {
		limit = { # Gor Vazumbrog
			owner = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = I14 } }
			OR = {
			   has_province_modifier = gor_vazumbrog_dauvek_veker_secure_road
			   has_province_modifier = gor_vazumbrog_dauvek_veker_caves_cleared
			}
		}
		dauvek_veker_colony_finished = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { tag = Z43 has_country_flag = harvesting_connadh } } #Aelnar
		province_event = { id = aelnar.103 }
	}
	#Drozma tur last stand win the siege of svemel, mostly for AI
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = drozma_last_stand_prov_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				from = {
					tag = REB
				}
				owner = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = drozma_fighting_last_stand
						overlord = {
							has_country_flag = drozma_fighting_last_stand
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { country_event = { id = ynn_events.27 } }
		}
	}

	if = {	#Brelar civil war for if ur a schizo and didn't make any subjects
		limit = {
			owner = {
				tag = G27
			}
		}
		g27_civil_war_end_lost_effect = yes
	}

	# G53 - Empkeios Slave Rebellion win
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = G53
					tag = U27
				}
				has_country_flag = G53_Slave_Rebellion
			}
			NOT = {
				FROM  = {
					num_of_rebel_armies = 1
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				FROM = {
					num_of_rebel_controlled_provinces = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = G53
			}
			G53 = {
				country_event = {
					id = empkeios_events.1306
				}
			}
		} 
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = U27
					U27 = {
						was_tag = G53
					}
				}
				U27 = {
					country_event = {
						id = empkeios_events.1306
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
	}

	#L01 Kuiika MT vs L13 Gomuvuri
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = kuiika_threatens_us
			FROM = {
				tag = L01
			}
		}
		L01 = {
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_kuiika.6
			 }
		}
	}
	if = { #Karakhanbar Disaster
		limit = { 
			has_province_modifier = karakhanbar_feyinfused_grove
			has_province_modifier = scorched_earth 
		}
		remove_province_modifier = karakhanbar_feyinfused_grove
	}
	if = { #Bonecarver
        limit = {
			owned_by = Z20
			FROM = { 
				tag = B27 
				ai = no
				is_in_war = {
					defender_leader = Z20
					attackers = B27
				}
				OR = {
					war_score_against = {
						who = Z20
						value = 90
					}
					Z20 = {
						all_owned_province = {
							controlled_by = B27
						}
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { is_year = 1500 }
			Z20 = { ai = yes }
        }
		B27 = {
			country_event = { id = flavour_bonecarver.18 }
		}

    }
	if = { #Escanni WoC Slaughter
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = escanni_wars_global_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = escanni_wars_end_global_flag }
			owner = {
				country_can_participate_in_escanni_wars = yes
			}
			NOT = { 
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = escanni_wars_slaughter
				}
			}
			NOT = { owner = { FROM = { alliance_with = PREV } } }
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = B34
					tag = B39
					tag = B54
					tag = Z51
					has_country_modifier = monstrous_nation
					ruler_is_witch_king = yes
				}
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25
			province_event = { id = escanni_wars.301 }
		}
	}

	if = {	#vizier challenge war
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = raja_new_castle
			has_saved_global_event_target = raj_vizier_global_target
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = has_vizier_won } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = raja_castle_not_ours
		}
		event_target:raj_vizier_global_target = {
			country_event = { id = rahenraj.5001 }
		}
		clr_province_flag = raja_new_castle
	}
	#Great Storm
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = I80_storm_wake_flag
				OR = {
					has_cast_shock_and_awe = yes
					has_cast_elemental_fury = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = I80_storm_wake
			duration = 1095
		}
	}
	else = {
		remove_province_modifier = I80_storm_wake
	}
	
	# Province control changes from Varamhar -> Nansalen, when Nansalen attacks Ayarallen.
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			owner = { 
				tag = F27
				is_in_war = { attacker_leader = F80 defender_leader = F27 }
			}
			region = harpy_hills_region
			controller = {
				is_in_war = { attacker_leader = F80 defender_leader = F27 }
			}
			F80 = { ai = no }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				controller = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = F80_cflag_will_aid_nansalen
						AND = {
							is_subject = yes
							overlord = { has_country_flag = F80_cflag_will_aid_nansalen }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			change_controller = F80
		}
		else = { # Other war participants may hand province occupations over to Varamhar, if so, hand them over.
			province_event = { id = flavor_nansalen.101 days = 30 }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { 
			FROM = { has_country_flag = RSP_trollshaunt_the_army_of_the_wretched_effect }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = RSP_trollshaunt_dreaded_mist }
			remove_province_modifier = RSP_trollshaunt_dreaded_mist
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = { NOT = { owned_by = FROM } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = RSP_trollshaunt_lesser_dreaded_mist
					duration = 730
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_province_modifier = RSP_trollshaunt_lesser_dreaded_mist }
			remove_province_modifier = RSP_trollshaunt_lesser_dreaded_mist
		}
	}
}

# province
# root = location, from = country that abandons colony
# Fired right before the colony is abandoned.
on_abandon_colony = {
	if = {
		limit = { # Gor Vazumbrog
			owner = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = I14 } }
			OR = {
			   has_province_modifier = gor_vazumbrog_dauvek_veker_secure_road
			   has_province_modifier = gor_vazumbrog_dauvek_veker_caves_cleared
			}
		}
		dauvek_veker_colony_finished = yes
	}
}

# province
# root = location, from = country that owns it
# Fired right after the great project is constructed
on_great_project_constructed = {
	remove_province_modifier = reveria_golden_dome_leviathan
	remove_province_modifier = the_dilapidated_court
	remove_province_modifier = the_dilapidated_court_2
	remove_province_modifier = bastion_in_the_mists
	remove_province_modifier = bastion_in_the_mists_2
	remove_province_modifier = they_watch_in_the_dark
	FROM = {
		if = { #Dragon Turtles
			limit = { tag_allowed_dragon_turtle_system = yes }
			dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = maxele_iron_hearted amount = 20 }
			dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = monzaketzya amount = 20 }
			dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = maruvarax amount = 20 }
		}
	}
}

				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

		limit = {
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = S93 }
			NOT = { has_ruler_flag = alefisol }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rinta_seeker_events.213
			days = 32
		}
	}

	if = { #Sareyand Monks
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_reform = sareyand_exorcist_priests_in_the_army
				has_reform = sareyand_pe_jaherian_exorcist_priests
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = one_xia.4
		}
	}

	#Great Storm Thing (Again. Of course)
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = I80_emulant_heir }
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = I80_emulant
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
	if = { #Salla Elyn mt
		limit = {
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = I26 } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = I26_dirwn_gosgeiddig_consort }

			if = {
				limit = { is_female = yes }
				define_consort = {
					culture = wood_elf
					name = "Dirwn"
					dynasty = "Gosgeidigg"
					male = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				define_consort = {
					culture = wood_elf
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = I26_dirwn_gosgeiddig_consort
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = I26_farwen_is_cruel
					has_country_flag = I26_farwen_is_righteous
					has_country_flag = I26_farwen_is_malevolent
					has_country_flag = I26_farwen_is_benevolent
				}
				has_ruler_flag = I26_is_farwen
			}
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_salla_elyn.400
				days = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = I26_cruel_farwen_modifier
					has_country_modifier = I26_malevolent_farwen_modifier
				}
				NOT = { has_ruler_flag = I26_is_farwen }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = I26_cruel_farwen_modifier
			remove_country_modifier = I26_malevolent_farwen_modifier
		}
	}
	#Badakhan
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = badakhan_heirs_bonus
		}
		country_event = {
			id = flavour_badakhan.200
		}
	}

	#Tsukqiao
	if = { #Might and Right
		limit = { has_reform = tsukqiao_throne_of_lies_reform }

			limit = {
				has_ruler_flag = tsukqiao_harimar_the_ruler_flag
			}

			add_legitimacy = -40
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = tsukqiao_might_and_right_upgrade_2 }

			add_legitimacy = -70
		}

		}
		else = {

		}
	}

	if = {

		}

		# - Hemantsen I dynasty buff check
		if = {

				mission_completed = R54_the_iron_heart

				NOT = { dynasty = "of the Iron Stripe" }
			}
			remove_country_modifier = R54_rule_of_the_iron_raja
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = R54_rule_of_the_iron_raja }
				dynasty = "of the Iron Stripe"
			}
			add_country_modifier = { 
				name = R54_rule_of_the_iron_raja 
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	# Brick Esthil MT if Varina dies (without being a Lich)
	if = { limit = { tag = B54 NOT = { ruler_is_lich = yes } has_country_flag = B54_cflag_varina_was_made_ruler } 
		B54_se_brick_MT = yes
	}

	#Dragon Turtle
	dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = haomake amount = 10 }
}

on_new_consort = {

	#apply correct racial flags
	update_consort_racial_flag = yes

	country_event = { id = consort_events.2 }
	#harpy consorts - UPDATE WHEN HARPY CULTURES ARE ADDED
	if = {
		limit = {
			consort_is_harpy = yes
			has_female_consort = no
		}
		clear_fast_consort_flags = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = F49
					was_tag = F49
				}
			}
			set_consort_culture = desert_elf
			set_consort_flag = elven_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = firanyan_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = gelkar
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = siadunan_harpy
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					set_consort_culture = surani
				}
				50 = {
					set_consort_culture = ghankedhen
				}
			}
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = pezarangi_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = sikai
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = semifire_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = hinphat
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = stonewing_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = khasani
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = jarnklo_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = olavish
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = naleni_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = metobesebi
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = reishao_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = wolf_command
			set_consort_flag = hobgoblin_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = kiohan_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = thamvoii
			set_consort_flag = ruinborn_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = nuzenapu_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = eagle_command
			set_consort_flag = hobgoblin_consort
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				consort_culture = nuraryi_harpy
			}
			set_consort_culture = beikling
			set_consort_flag = human_consort
		}
	}
	country_event = { id = anb_ruler.100 } # long lived consort
	# must happen after the harpy consort setting stuff above

	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = had_10_years_anniversary }
		clr_ruler_flag = had_10_years_anniversary
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = had_20_years_anniversary }
		clr_ruler_flag = had_20_years_anniversary
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = consort_had_affection_of_ruler }
		clr_ruler_flag = consort_had_affection_of_ruler
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = sought_after_bachelor }
		remove_country_modifier = sought_after_bachelor
	}
	if = {
		limit = { consort_is_powerful_mage = yes }
		add_ruler_modifier = { name = consort_mage_personality_mod duration = -1 }
	}
	else = { remove_country_modifier = consort_mage_personality_mod }

	#Duwarkani gov reform

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_reform = winged_menkaunswt_reform
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				consort_adm = 4
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = duwarkani_admin_consort
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				consort_dip = 4
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = duwarkani_diplo_consort
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				consort_mil = 4
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = duwarkani_mil_consort
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	#themarenn ryala path
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			OR = { tag = A95 was_tag = A95 } ai = no has_country_flag = a95_ryalan_prosperity 
		} 
		themarenn_refresh_prosperity = yes 
		themarenn_ryala_prosperity = yes
	}
}

	}

	update_ruler_racial_flag = yes
	
	#Zodiac update using heir
	if = { 
		limit = {
			OR = {
				religion = ynn_river_worship
				religion = ynn_river_reformed
			}
		}
		heir_ynn_zodiac = yes
	}

	#Heir is mage modifier
	if = {
		limit = { has_heir_flag = is_powerful_mage }
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = heir_mage_personality_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	#Malacnar Regency
	if = {
		limit = { tag = G32 }
		country_event = { id = flavor_malacnar.9 days = 1 }
	}
}

			has_reform = matriarchal_pirate_republic

	events = {

# country
on_bankruptcy = {
	events = {
		racial_modifiers.5		#Racial admin change if unmatching
		flavour_ovdal_tungr.60 	# Ovdal Tungr bankruptcy bailout
	}
	clear_roadwarrior_modifiers = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = roadwarrior_great_convoy }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = roadwarrior_main_1
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	#hoardcurse modifier
	remove_country_modifier = the_reformist
	# Anbennar - bankruptcy doesn't trigger on_loan_repaid, so "indebted to..." privileges aren't revoked unless checked here
    on_loan_repaid_estate_privileges_effect = yes
	set_country_flag = has_gone_bankrupt
	if = { # house of rags easteregg
		limit = { tag = B09 }
		override_country_name = HOUSE_OF_RAGS
	}
}

# country (country annexing, root = target)
on_diplomatic_annex = {
	events = {
		610
	}

	#Mulen cancel income transfer
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { tag = F47 } }
		country_event = { id = flavour_mulen.24 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = F72 }
		5434 = { remove_province_modifier = mulen_trade_from_kvangraak }
		5460 = { remove_trade_modifier = { who = FROM key = mulen_trade_from_kvangraak } }
	}
	if = { #prophecy of no annex good ending
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = taychendi_vassal_prophecy_vassal }
		}
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = taychendi_vassal_prophecy_vassal }
		country_event = { id = taychendi.18 }
	}
	if = { #istralore subject elector 
		limit = {
			is_or_was_tag = {
				tag = A45
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = A31
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = A45_justified_vassal_A31
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = A33
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = A45_justified_vassal_A33
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = A73
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = A45_justified_vassal_A73
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					tag = A77
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = A45_justified_vassal_A77
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				tag = Z91
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = taric_option_c
		clr_country_flag = taric_option_d
		set_country_flag = taric_option_b
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			from = {
				tag = Z92
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = cagodic_option_c
		clr_country_flag = cagodic_option_d
		set_country_flag = cagodic_option_b
	}

	#Deranne
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			FROM = {
				tag = A21
			}
			has_country_flag = deranne_integrate_venail_flag
		}
		country_event = {
			id = flavour_deranne.34
		}
	}
	if = { 
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = deranne_fahvanosy_vassal }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_4
			}
			remove_country_modifier = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_4
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_3 
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_3
			}
			remove_country_modifier = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_3
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_2
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_2
			}
			remove_country_modifier = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_2
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_1
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_country_modifier = deranne_agreement_with_high_priestess_1
		}
	}

	#Fangaulan Pantheon
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = fangaulan_pantheon_kanhati_poem
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					total_development = 50
				}
			}
			add_adm_power = 25
			add_dip_power = 25
			add_mil_power = 25
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = enchantment_3_harpy_mod
			religion = the_hunt
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			which = vassalDev
			value = trigger_value:total_development
			who = FROM
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			which = vassalDev
			value = 3
		}
		var_effect = {
			effect = add_church_power
			var = vassalDev
			sign = +
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_fogharkarn_palace_privilege
		}
		add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			desc = fogharkarn_palace_fest
			loyalty = 20
			duration = 1460
		}
	}
}

# country
on_heir_death = {
	events = {
		flavor_duwarkani.4 #Duwarkani failsafe
	}
	country_event = { id = hisost.98 days = 1 } #hisost yamok new heirs
	if = { #Delayed because elective heirs doesn't show up immediately
		limit = { has_reform = magisterium_reform }
		country_event = { id = flavor_magisterium.23 days = 3 } #Mage for Non-Vinerick heir
		country_event = { id = flavor_magisterium.29 days = 3 } #Mage for Vinerick heir
	}
	magic_on_heir_death = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = heir_dip_education }
		clr_country_flag = heir_dip_education
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = heir_mil_education }
		clr_country_flag = heir_mil_education
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = heir_adm_education }
		clr_country_flag = heir_adm_education
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = well_advised_tutored_heir }
		clr_ruler_flag = well_advised_tutored_heir
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = heir_went_on_grand_tour }
		clr_ruler_flag = heir_went_on_grand_tour
	}
	#if = {
		#limit = { has_country_flag = albrecht_achilles_flag }
		#clr_country_flag = albrecht_achilles_flag #Death of original Albrecht Achilles
	#}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = sancaga_cikma }
		clr_ruler_flag = sancaga_cikma
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = heir_in_training
			}
			remove_province_modifier = heir_in_training
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_ruler_flag = returned_from_sancaga_sikma_province }
		clr_ruler_flag = returned_from_sancaga_sikma_province
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = teplinbasiet_arena_kingdom_reform }
		clr_country_flag = Y58_allied_noble_won
		clr_country_flag = Y58_local_fighter_won
		clr_country_flag = Y58_prominent_dauloph_won
		clr_country_flag = Y58_relative_won
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_reform = tagharoghi_reform
				has_reform = demon_empire_reform
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = oni_heir_shinukhorchi
		clr_country_flag = oni_heir_chumijemoya
		clr_country_flag = oni_heir_ajgriijarul
		clr_country_flag = oni_heir_kabiurgarko
		clr_country_flag = oni_heir_khelorvalshi
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = male_harpy_begone #male harpy replacement - see on_new_heir
		}
		country_event = {
			id = harpy_events.301
		}
	}
	#the hunt setup
	remove_country_modifier = harpy_myna_doctrine_heir
	remove_country_modifier = harpy_crane_doctrine_heir
	remove_country_modifier = harpy_eagle_doctrine_heir


	clr_country_flag = theo_local_noble_flag #Anbennar - Fix for bugged devotion events due to being incompatible/ineligible with the same heir selection event
	clr_country_flag = theo_foreign_noble_flag
	clr_country_flag = theo_merchants_son_flag
	clr_country_flag = theo_talented_theologian_flag
	clr_country_flag = theo_local_preacher_flag

	if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_mongoose_shifter
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_leopard_shifter
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_elephant_shifter
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = heir_is_mongoose_shifter
        remove_country_modifier = heir_is_leopard_shifter
        remove_country_modifier = heir_is_elephant_shifter
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = Z18
			has_country_flag = marosh_in_corintar
		}
		country_event = { id = flavor_frozenmaw.15 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = goblinic_shamanism
			has_any_heir_cult_active = yes
		}
		remove_heir_cult = yes
	}
	if = { #Salla Elyn mt
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = I26_dirwn_gosgeiddig_consort
		}
		clr_country_flag = I26_dirwn_gosgeiddig_consort
	}
	#Badakhan
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = badakhan_heirs_bonus
		}
		country_event = {
			id = flavour_badakhan.200
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = keladora_got }
		add_casus_belli = {
			target = F21
			type = cb_restore_personal_union
			months = 120
		}
		clr_country_flag = keladora_got
	}


	#Orenvalyam
	remove_country_modifier = U39_heir_monasticist
	remove_country_modifier = U39_heir_kavalalist
	remove_country_modifier = U39_heir_kamrayakvalist
	if = { #Lelanan MT
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = L36_kyola_leading_spouses_crusade
		}
		country_event = { id = flavour_lelanan.6 }
	}
}

# country
on_new_heir = {
	events = {
		dragon_turtles.17
	}
	if = {
		limit = { religion = goblinic_shamanism }
		if = {
			limit = { has_any_heir_cult_active = yes }
			remove_heir_cult = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = enabled_cult_for_heirs
			}
			country_event = {
				id = goblinic_shamanism_flavor.3
			}
		}
	}

	#apply correct racial flags
	update_heir_racial_flag = yes

	country_event = { id = racial_misc.1 days = 2 }		# Half-orc heirs for cross-racial marriages
	country_event = { id = racial_misc.2 days = 2 }		# Half-elf heirs for cross-racial marriages
	country_event = { id = racial_misc.3 days = 2 }		# Human heirs for half-elf human marriages
	country_event = { id = racial_misc.4 days = 2 }		# Harpy heirs for harpy marriages
	country_event = { id = racial_misc.10 days = 1 }	# Heirs are set to their parents race since event heirs are given primary culture instead
	country_event = { id = rahenraj.6 days = 5 }		# Replace heir if incorrect race for Senapti
	country_event = { id = anb_ruler.101 days = 3 }		# Immortal/long-lived trait
	country_event = { id = magic_system.19 days = 3 }	# Always-mage nations get mage heirs
	if = { limit = { heir_is_harpy = yes }	
		if = { limit = { has_female_heir = no } #male harpy replacement
			set_country_flag = male_harpy_begone #this triggers an if clause in on_heir_death - RNG is fixed in this on_action so to generate randomly statted heirs they need to be made elsewhere.
			kill_heir = { allow_new_heir = no }	
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = harpy_events.102 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				religion = gods_of_the_taychend
				religion = gods_of_the_taychend_reformed
			}
		}
		if = {	
			limit = { has_ruler_flag = had_birth_ceremony }
			random = {
				chance = 10
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = taychendi.13 } }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 30
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = taychendi.13 } }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_reform = trust_of_the_future
		}
		ROOT = { country_event = { id = flavour_counts_league.30 } }
	}
	#Heir is mage modifier
	if = {
		limit = { heir_is_powerful_mage = yes }
		add_ruler_modifier = { name = heir_mage_personality_mod duration = -1 }
	}
	else = { remove_country_modifier = heir_mage_personality_mod }
	if = { 
		limit = {
			OR = { tag = A95 was_tag = A95 } ai = no has_country_flag = a95_esmaryal_heir_education
		} 
		country_event = { id = flavour_themarenn.43 } 
	} #themarenn esmaryal path

	if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_mongoose_shifter
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_leopard_shifter
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_elephant_shifter
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = heir_is_mongoose_shifter
        remove_country_modifier = heir_is_leopard_shifter
        remove_country_modifier = heir_is_elephant_shifter
	}
	# if = { limit = { tag = I27 }
	# 	# country_event = { id = flavour_salla_myna.2 } # The Newest Myna, May 3 2026 - Disabled due lacking loc
	# }

	if = { #You got a new heir, but you're currently doing a vampire/lich revival
		limit = { has_country_flag = in_revival_heir }
		clr_country_flag = in_revival_heir
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = vampire_ruler_female
					has_country_flag = lich_ruler_female
				}
			}
			define_heir = { age = 30 female = yes max_random_adm = 0 max_random_dip = 0 max_random_mil = 0 hide_skills = yes }
		}
		else = {
			define_heir = { age = 30 male = yes max_random_adm = 0 max_random_dip = 0 max_random_mil = 0 hide_skills = yes }
		}
		set_country_flag = in_revival_heir
	}

	if = {
		limit = { 
			mission_completed = seinathil_modernize_college
			has_regency = no
			heir_is_not_powerful_mage = yes
		}
		country_event = { id = seinathil.16 days = 3650 random = 365 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_reform = jinnakah_ardimyan_vizierate
		}
		country_event = { id = planetouched.105 }
	}

	if = { #Salla elyn mt
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = I26_cruel_farwen_modifier
				has_country_modifier = I26_malevolent_farwen_modifier
			}
			NOT = { has_ruler_flag = I26_is_farwen }
		}
		remove_country_modifier = I26_cruel_farwen_modifier
		remove_country_modifier = I26_malevolent_farwen_modifier
	}

	if = { #Harpy Tolerance Event 'Harpy Wife, Happy Life' Effect
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = harpy_tolerance_harpy_wife_happy_life
		}
		add_heir_claim = -20
		clr_country_flag = harpy_tolerance_harpy_wife_happy_life
	}
}

# Emperor from same dynasty
on_successive_emperor = {
	emperor = {
		save_global_event_target_as = Emperor
		#Anbennar - Emperor won't denounce themselves
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = denounced_witch_king
			}
			remove_country_modifier = denounced_witch_king
		}
	}
	events = {
		900
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			emperor = { ai = yes }
		}
		add_imperial_influence = 5
	}
}

# Called whenever a new emperor is elected
# FROM = Previous Emperor
# ROOT = New Emperor
on_emperor_elected = {
	every_elector = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				preferred_emperor = root
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = supported_successive_emperors
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				which = supported_successive_emperors
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}

	emperor = {
		save_global_event_target_as = Emperor
		country_event = { id = long_lived_emperor.1 }
	}

	if = { #Salt and Silence
        limit = {
            has_global_flag = war_of_salt_and_silence 
            has_saved_global_event_target = salt_and_silence_emperor
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:salt_and_silence_emperor = { 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = currently_in_salt_silence_war }
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				save_global_event_target_as = salt_and_silence_emperor
			}
        }
    }
	if = { #Stops the Salt and Silence incident if the Giant is elected during the incident - Edgecase
		limit = {
			active_imperial_incident = any #This is required or this triggers a CTD on emperor change
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				active_imperial_incident = incident_salt_and_silence
				tag = event_target:salt_and_silence_giant
			}
			set_imperial_incident = none
			event_target:salt_and_silence_giant = {
				country_event = {
					id = flavor_salt_silence_incident.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #istralore
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				is_or_was_tag = {
					tag = A45
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_country_modifier = A45_istralari_commanders
				}
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					is_part_of_hre = yes
					religion = corinite
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = A45_istralari_commanders
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_country_flag = A45_victory_on_halann_flag
				}
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = {
					is_part_of_hre = yes
					religion = corinite
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = A45_victory_on_halann
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = A45_Aucanna_retired }
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				country_event = {
					id = istralore.38
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = diet_occupied }
			remove_country_modifier = diet_occupied
			ROOT = {
				add_country_modifier = { name = diet_occupied duration = -1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						modifier = opinion_imperial_diplomacy
						who = prev
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						modifier = opinion_imperial_diplomacy
						who = prev
					}
				}
				reverse_remove_opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_imperial_diplomacy
					who = prev
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_imperial_diplomacy
						who = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { A77 = { is_subject_of_type = imperial_bodyguard } }
		if = {
			limit = { 
				A77 = {
					is_elector = yes
					ROOT = {
						NOT = { has_country_modifier = A77_preatorian_electors }
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				remove_country_modifier = A77_preatorian_electors
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = A77_preatorian_electors
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_country_modifier = supporting_orda_aldresia
			free_vassal = A77
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = supporting_orda_aldresia
				duration = -1
			}
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = imperial_bodyguard
				subject = A77
			}
		} 
	}

	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = has_global_flag
		LRM_PTL_8 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_8 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_7 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_7 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_6 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_6 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_5 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_5 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_4 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_4 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_3 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_3 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_2 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_2 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_1 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_1 duration = -1 } }
		LRM_PTL_0 = { add_ruler_modifier = { name = LRM_privilege_of_the_luna_0 duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
	}
	FROM = {
		remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_modifier_tier_3
		remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_modifier_tier_2
		remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_modifier_tier_1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			8 = {
				has_great_project = {
					type = imperial_palace_anbenncost
					tier = 1
				}
				owner = { is_part_of_hre = yes }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_1
			remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_2
			remove_country_modifier = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				8 = {
					has_great_project = {
						type = imperial_palace_anbenncost
						tier = 3
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = imperial_palace_modifier_tier_3
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_part_of_hre = yes }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_3
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				8 = {
					has_great_project = {
						type = imperial_palace_anbenncost
						tier = 2
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = imperial_palace_modifier_tier_2
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_part_of_hre = yes }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_2
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			ROOT = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = imperial_palace_modifier_tier_1
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_part_of_hre = yes }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = imperial_palace_prince_modifier_tier_1
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			hre_reform_passed = anbennar_internal_divisions
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_part_of_hre = yes
			}
			refresh_court_bonus = yes
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			hre_reform_passed = anbennar_expand_marquis_rank
			NOT = { tag = Z01 }
		}
		emperor = {
			country_event = { id = flavour_eoa_reforms.6 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	if = {
        limit = {
            hre_reform_passed = anbennar_internal_divisions
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                emperor = { has_reform = damerian_monarchy }
            }
            emperor = {
                add_government_reform = damerian_monarchy_aristo_path
            }
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { emperor = { has_reform = imperial_parliament_reform } }
            }
            emperor = { #just to make sure they always have it and jank doesnt happen
                add_government_reform = imperial_parliament_reform
            }
        }
    }
	#Pashaine
	if = {
		limit = { tag = B59 }
		country_event = { id = flavour_pashaine.1024 days = 15 }
	}
}
