# Nation annexed.
# FROM is the nation being annexed
on_annexed = {
	events = {
		# celestial_empire_events.1 # Empire dismantled
	}
	on_annexed_estate_privileges_effect = yes
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = { # conquered the ravelian state
				tag = Z97
			}
			ROOT = {
				capital_scope = {
					province_event = {
						id = ravelian.1002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { # conquered Silentblade
				tag = I43
			}
			ROOT = {
				country_event = {
					id = flavour_cursed_howl.11
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_emperor_of_china = yes }
			dismantle_empire_of_china = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = legatus_natus }
			remove_country_modifier = legatus_natus
			set_global_flag = no_legatus_natus
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = primas_germaniae }
			remove_country_modifier = primas_germaniae
			set_global_flag = no_primas_germaniae
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_companion = yes
					mission_completed = G32_with_two_companions
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = G32_companions_active
		}
		if = {	#Can't inherit Ynnic Iosahar by annexing their Overlord unless you're a Ynnic Overlord
			limit = { ynnic_iosahar = 1 }
			every_subject_country = {
				country_event = { id = ynn_events.19 }
			}
		}

		#transfer dwarovkron fragments
		if = {
			limit = { has_dwarovkron_fragment = yes }
			transfer_dwarovkron_fragments = yes
		}

		#honderaak incident, Xanzerbexis annexed
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = A49
				OR = {
					364 = { owner = { NOT = { culture_group = gnollish } is_part_of_hre = no } }
					6513 = { owner = { NOT = { culture_group = gnollish } is_part_of_hre = no } }
					377 = { owner = { NOT = { culture_group = gnollish } is_part_of_hre = no } }
					375 = { owner = { NOT = { culture_group = gnollish } is_part_of_hre = no } }
				}
			}
			ROOT = { country_event = { id = flavor_honderaak.1 days = 2 } }
		}

		#Mulen cancel income transfer
		if = {
			limit = { tag = F47 }
			ROOT = { country_event = { id = flavour_mulen.24 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = F72 }
			5434 = { remove_province_modifier = mulen_trade_from_kvangraak }
			5460 = { remove_trade_modifier = { who = FROM key = mulen_trade_from_kvangraak } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = A77 }
			emperor = {
				remove_country_modifier = supporting_orda_aldresia
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = current_aakhet_host }
			aakhet_reset = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = federation_leader }
			clr_country_flag = federation_leader
			random_country = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = lake_federation_member is_subject = no }
				country_event = { id = lake.102 days = 1 }
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_sri_baginda = yes }
			remove_sri_baginda = yes
			ROOT = { make_random_highest_prestige_sri_baginda = yes }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = lakeInvestment
					value = 1
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = lakeInvestment
					which = 4000
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = federation_assembly_house_build }
			}
			4000 = {
				set_variable = {
					which = lakeInvestment
					value = 0
				}
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = lake_federation_member }
				4000 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = lakeInvestment
									which = PREV
								}
							}
						}
						set_variable = {
							which = lakeInvestment
							which = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = lakeInvestmentBank
					value = 1
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = lakeInvestmentBank
					which = 4000
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = federation_central_bank_build }
			}
			4000 = {
				set_variable = {
					which = lakeInvestmentBank
					value = 0
				}
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = lake_federation_member }
				4000 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = lakeInvestmentBank
									which = PREV
								}
							}
						}
						set_variable = {
							which = lakeInvestmentBank
							which = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = museumInvestment
					value = 1
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = museumInvestment
					which = 4000
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = federation_museum_build }
			}
			4000 = {
				set_variable = {
					which = museumInvestment
					value = 0
				}
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = lake_federation_member }
				4000 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								check_variable = {
									which = museumInvestment
									which = PREV
								}
							}
						}
						set_variable = {
							which = museumInvestment
							which = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_saved_global_event_target = mangrove_leader }
			if = {
				limit = { tag = event_target:mangrove_leader }
				mangrove_new_leader_on_annexed = yes
			}
		}
	}
	# okman:
	# if the tag was annexed by nobody - for example it was destroyed by decolonisation
	# then THIS is not set to anything, and we have to scope to ROOT manually to force a failure and avoid errors
	ROOT = {
		if = { #Shuvuush MT flags (duplicated in on war won)
			limit = {
				has_mission = shuvuush_surrounded_cornered
				FROM = { capital_scope = { superregion = yanshen_superregion } }
			}
			set_country_flag = shuvuush_won_yanshen_war
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_mission = shuvuush_rule_steppe
				FROM = { religion = saanorgegh }
			}
			set_country_flag = shuvuush_won_saanorgegh_war
		}

		if = {
			limit = { current_age = age_of_discovery }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_modifier = monstrous_nation } }
				set_country_flag = annexed_monstrous
			}
			else = { set_country_flag = annexed_non_monstrous }
		}

		#Venomtooth Adventurer killing events
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { tag = B22 } }
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = B03 } }
				country_event = {
					id = flavor_venomtooth.100
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = B10 } }
				country_event = {
					id = flavor_venomtooth.101
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = B07 } }
				country_event = {
					id = flavor_venomtooth.102
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = B11 } }
				country_event = {
					id = flavor_venomtooth.103
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_country_modifier = gaafhlids_scrolls_legacy_modifier } }
		clr_global_flag = found_gaafhlids_scrolls_legacy_fl
		FROM = {
			remove_country_modifier = gaafhlids_scrolls_legacy_modifier
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_country_modifier = bajnmra_sextant_legacy_modifier } }
		clr_global_flag = found_bajnmra_sextant_legacy_fl
		FROM = {
			remove_country_modifier = bajnmra_sextant_legacy_modifier
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {FROM = { has_country_modifier = L37_the_bottle_of_nyeekayba } }
		clr_global_flag = found_bottle_of_nyeekayba_legacy_fl
		FROM = {
			remove_country_modifier = L37_the_bottle_of_nyeekayba
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_country_modifier = faasas_legacy_modifier } }
		clr_global_flag = found_faasas_legacy_fl
		FROM = {
			remove_country_modifier = faasas_legacy_modifier
		}
	}
	# Yenbenmirra CoF redistribution
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_reform = yenbenmirra_tribe
				check_variable = {
					which = children_of_fire_count
					value = 200
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = { has_reform = yenbenmirra_tribe }
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				overlord = {
					change_variable = {
						which = children_of_fire_count
						which = FROM
					}
					yenbenmirra_update_cof_modifier = yes #scripted effect can be edited in the anb_scripted_effects_for_insyaa file
					yenbenmirra_update_hinui_hunters = { target_scope = capital_scope }
					country_event = { id = yenbenmirra.12 }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						has_reform = yenbenmirra_tribe
						NOT = { tag = FROM }
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = children_of_fire_count
						which = FROM
					}
					yenbenmirra_update_cof_modifier = yes #scripted effect can be edited in the anb_scripted_effects_for_insyaa file
					yenbenmirra_update_hinui_hunters = { target_scope = capital_scope }
					country_event = { id = yenbenmirra.12 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#AnbennarNewVer - change this to khetaratan yo
# When a nation gains the Mandate of Heaven (becomes the Emperor of China)
# FROM = Old Emperor, ROOT = New Emperor
on_mandate_of_heaven_gained = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = empire_of_china_dismantled }
		dismantle_empire_of_china = no
	}
	save_global_event_target_as = EmperorOfChina
	set_mandate = 60
	remove_country_modifier = mandate_lost_steward
	add_country_modifier = {
		name = mandate_new_steward
		duration = 7300
	}
	country_event = { id = khet_mandate.01 }
	kheterata_region = {
		limit = { NOT = { is_core = ROOT } }
		add_permanent_claim = ROOT
	}
	mothers_sorrow_group = {
		limit = { NOT = { is_core = ROOT } }
		add_permanent_claim = ROOT
	}
	update_sorrow_province_count = yes
	set_meritocracy = 50
	if = {
		limit = { any_subject_country = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state_anb } }
		#Reset the gnoll trib count variable
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { gnoll_tributary_bonus_count = 1 } }
            set_variable = { gnoll_tributary_bonus_count = 0 }
        }
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state_anb }
			country_event = { id = khet_mandate.02 } 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = U01 } #kheterata
		restore_country_name = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ai = yes }
		475 = { add_core = ROOT }
		473 = { add_core = ROOT }
		463 = { add_core = ROOT }
		479 = { add_core = ROOT }
		5481 = { add_core = ROOT }
	}
}

# When a nation loses the Mandate of Heaven
# FROM = New Emperor, ROOT = Old Emperor
on_mandate_of_heaven_lost = {
	#set_government_rank = 2
	remove_country_modifier = mandate_new_steward
	add_country_modifier = {
		name = mandate_lost_steward
		duration = 7300	# 20 years
	}
	add_stability = -2
	kheterata_region = {
		limit = { is_permanent_claim = ROOT }
		remove_claim = ROOT
	}
	mothers_sorrow_group = {
		limit = { is_permanent_claim = ROOT }
		remove_claim = ROOT
	}
	clr_mandate_modifiers = yes
	if = {
		limit = { any_subject_country = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state } }
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state }
			country_event = { id = khet_mandate.03 } 
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = {
				tag = U02 #nirat
				tag = U04 #aakheta
				tag = L28 #koroshesh
			}
		}
		restore_country_name = yes
	}
	475 = { remove_core = ROOT }
	473 = { remove_core = ROOT }
	463 = { remove_core = ROOT }
	479 = { remove_core = ROOT }
	5481 = { remove_core = ROOT }
}

on_embrace_revolution = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_subject_country = {
				has_country_modifier = colony_inspired_by_revolution
			}
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			remove_country_modifier = colony_inspired_by_revolution
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { government = republic } }
		change_government = republic
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			revolution_target_exists = no
			is_great_power = yes
		}
		set_revolution_target = ROOT
		add_government_reform = revolutionary_republic_reform
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = last_revolutionary_country
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = last_revolutionary_country
				}
				clr_country_flag = last_revolutionary_country
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_government_reform = junior_revolutionary_republic_reform
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = parliamentary_reform }
		remove_government_reform = parliamentary_reform
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = Z01 }
		Z01 = {
			change_country_color = { color = { 60 56 56 } }
			override_country_name = BLACKPOWDER_ANBENNAR
		}
	}
	kill_ruler = yes
	set_country_flag = revolutionary_republic_flag
	set_country_flag = had_revolution
	if = {
		limit = { 
			4907 = {
				owner = { 
					mission_completed = Y15_light_liberty 
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Y15_light_at_worlds_end }
				}
			}
			all_country = {
				is_revolutionary = yes
			}
		}

		country_event = { id = flavor_beikdugang.101 }
	}
}

# THIS = Revolutionary country being beaten, FROM = Country enforcing the peace treaty
on_dismantle_revolution = {
	events = {
		center_of_revolution.1500
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_country = {
				has_country_flag = last_revolutionary_country
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = last_revolutionary_country
			}
			clr_country_flag = last_revolutionary_country
		}
	}
	set_country_flag = last_revolutionary_country
}

# province
on_adm_development = {
	on_adm_development_effect = yes
	on_development_effect = yes

	#Anbennar
	events = {
		kheionai.4
		flavour_mulen.1
		flavour_mulen.2
		flavour_gor_vazumbrog.201
	}

	if = { #vaengheim
		limit = {
			Z88 = {
				has_country_flag = Z88_subject_dev_refund 
			}
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = Z88
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = Z88_refund_cd
				}
			}
		}
		Z88 = {
			add_adm_power = 50
		}
		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Z88_refund_cd
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = Z88
				modifier = developed_subject_z88
			}
		}
	}
}

# province
on_dip_development = {
	on_dip_development_effect = yes
	on_development_effect = yes

	#Anbennar
	events = {
		kheionai.4
		flavour_mulen.1
		flavour_mulen.2
		flavour_gor_vazumbrog.201
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_U10_torment_of_hellfire }
			base_production = 10
			has_building = tradecompany
			trade_goods = slaves
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = U10_hellfire_factory
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = { #vaengheim
		limit = {
			Z88 = {
				has_country_flag = Z88_subject_dev_refund 
			}
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = Z88
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = Z88_refund_cd
				}
			}
		}
		Z88 = {
			add_dip_power = 50
		}
		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Z88_refund_cd
				hidden = yes
				duration = 1825
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = Z88
				modifier = developed_subject_z88
			}
		}
	}
}

# province
on_mil_development = {
	on_mil_development_effect = yes
	on_development_effect = yes

	#Anbennar
	events = {
		kheionai.4
		flavour_mulen.1
		flavour_mulen.2
		flavour_gor_vazumbrog.201
	}

	if = { #vaengheim
		limit = {
			Z88 = {
				has_country_flag = Z88_subject_dev_refund 
			}
			owner = {
				is_subject_of = Z88
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = Z88_refund_cd
				}
			}
		}
		Z88 = {
			add_mil_power = 50
		}
		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Z88_refund_cd
				duration = 1825
				hidden = yes
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = Z88
				modifier = developed_subject_z88
			}
		}
	}

	# Huugeta Mercenary Enterprise
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = S45_mercenary_enterprise
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = S45_mil_dev_counter
				value = 1
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = S45_mil_dev_counter
						value = 5
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = S45_mil_dev_counter
					value = 0
				}
				S45_add_momentum = { value = 1 action = dev }
			}
		}

		# Huugeta Mercenary Chapter
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = S45_mercenary_chapters }
				S45_mercenary_chapter_requirements = yes
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = S45_mercenary_chapter
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_estate = estate_planetouched ai = no }
			NOT = { has_province_flag = planetouched_improved_mil_dev_twice_flag }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = planetouched_improved_mil_dev_flag }
			set_province_flag = planetouched_improved_mil_dev_twice_flag
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = planetouchedImprovedMilDevQuan
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else = { set_province_flag = planetouched_improved_mil_dev_flag }
	}
}

					exists = yes
					war_with = ROOT
					any_owned_province = {
						controlled_by = root
					}
				}
				land_maintenance = 1.0
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = crusader duration = -1 }
		}
		else = {
			remove_country_modifier = crusader
		}
	}
	
	#defense of the empire triggered mod replacement
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			is_part_of_hre = yes
			hre_reform_passed = anbennar_imperial_war
			is_at_war = yes
			OR = {
				is_emperor = yes
				is_elector = yes
			}
			any_war_enemy_country = {
				NOT = { is_part_of_hre = yes }
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = defense_of_the_empire_modifier duration = -1 }
	}
	else = {
		remove_country_modifier = defense_of_the_empire_modifier
	}
	
	#counter revolution triggered mod replacement
	if = {
		limit = {
			revolution_target_exists = yes
			is_revolutionary = no
			is_free_or_tributary_trigger = yes
			government = monarchy
			revolution_target = {
				OR = {
					capital_scope = {
						continent = ROOT
					}
					is_neighbor_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				revolution_target = {
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = counter_revolution duration = -1 }
			remove_country_modifier = reaction
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = reaction duration = -1 }
			remove_country_modifier = counter_revolution
		}
	}
	else = {
		remove_country_modifier = reaction
		remove_country_modifier = counter_revolution
	}
	
	#imperial mage triggered mod replacement

	#Gronstunad Sovereign Authority
	if = {

				limit = {
					OR = {

							overlord = {
								reverse_has_opinion = {
									who = PREV
									value = 0
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = { add_government_power = { mechanic_type = gronstunad_authority_mechanic power_type = gronstunad_authority_power value = -2.0 } }
			}
			
			every_owned_province = {
				if = {
					limit = { devastation = 0.01 }
					ROOT = { add_government_power = { mechanic_type = gronstunad_authority_mechanic power_type = gronstunad_authority_power value = -0.02 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_prosperous = yes }
					ROOT = { add_government_power = { mechanic_type = gronstunad_authority_mechanic power_type = gronstunad_authority_power value = 0.03 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Charkuchin Kobold Supplies

		}

		# This is the one that starts decolonising if you're out of supplies
		country_event = {
			id = charkuchin_kobold.7
		}
	}

	#Monthly check to remove excommunication ravelian modifier
	#Context: Vanilla papacy relies on triggered modifiers to give out the excommunicated country modifier, but since anbennar
	#uses it for achievements it had to be moved to the diplo actions excommunicate_action and use a new modifier. So this should
	#function similarly to triggered modifiers.
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = ravelian 
			is_excommunicated = no
			has_country_modifier = ravelian_excommunicated
		}
		remove_country_modifier = ravelian_excommunicated
	}

	if ={
		limit = {
			tag = I19
			has_country_modifier = az_an_vurodrmonir_spell_infinite_visions_effect_mod
		}
		country_event = { 
			id = flavor_ovdal_az_an.106
		}
	}

	#check to see if eligible princes have mage personality (EoA)
	if = {
		limit = {
			hre_reform_passed = anbennar_nobles_of_the_wand
			is_part_of_hre = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ruler_is_not_powerful_mage = yes }
			add_country_modifier = {
				hidden = yes
				name = eoa_non_mage_malus
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_country_modifier = eoa_non_mage_malus
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_emperor = yes
			hre_reform_passed = anbennar_internal_divisions
		}
		country_event = { id = flavour_eoa_reforms.13 }
	}

	#Endhuvi mini disaster
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = R36_stagnant_water_active }
		country_event = { id = flavour_endhuvi.101 }
	}

	#Yezel Mora misery gain
	# I'm putting this here rather than adding monthly_misery_gain static modifiers for a few reasons:
	# 1. Stability and Unrest giving misery can be done, but devastation >= 90 cannot be done with just a
	#	modification to the devastation static modifier
	# 2. I could use a province triggered modifier for devastation, but then there would need to be that PTM
	#	on every Yezel Mora province, and the tooltip will show many, many instances of +X
	# 3. Since I need to use custom buttons for using the gov power, I need to use add_government_power for
	#	the cost, but that is affected by any misery_gain_modifiers, which is painful, so all of the scaling
	#	is done manually inside yezel_mora_misery_gain_scale_variable
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = S70
			OR = {
				has_government_mechanic = yezel_mora_misery_mechanic_t1
				has_government_mechanic = yezel_mora_misery_mechanic_t2
				has_government_mechanic = yezel_mora_misery_mechanic_t3
			}
		}
		yezel_mora_misery_monthly_gain = yes
	}

	#Lelanan Love gain
	# I'm putting this here rather than adding monthly_lelanan_love_power static modifiers because:
	#   -Expanded Infra and Prosperity giving love and devastation losing love can be done, but the tooltip generated for this quickly becomes
	#    *extremely* long, rendering it completely useless and an eyesore and preventing the player from checking their current Love amount.
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			ai = no
			has_government_mechanic = lelanan_love_mechanic
		}
		lelanan_love_monthly_gain = yes
	}

	ai_magic_siege_pulse = yes

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { army_size_percentage = 1.001 } }
		remove_country_modifier = mechanim_over_forcelimit
	}

	# Badakhan gov power
	if = {
		limit = { has_government_mechanic = badakhan_orcish_soul_mechanic }
		badakhan_monthly_power_gain = yes
	}

	if = { #Tsukqiao Might and Right
		limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = Z60 } }
		tsukqiao_calc_might_and_right_effect = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = mangrove_restart_voting }
		REB = {
			country_event = {
				id = mangrove.100
			}
		}
	}

	planetouched_land_share_equalizer_effect = yes

	if = {
		limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = H83 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_reform = H83_dream_dominion_reform
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_war_enemy_country = {
						culture_group = dwarven
					}
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = H83_dreamfire_dominion_at_war_with_dwarf
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = H83_dreamfire_dominion_at_war_with_dwarf }
				remove_country_modifier = H83_dreamfire_dominion_at_war_with_dwarf
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_reform = H83_dreamfire_crusade_reform
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = H83_upgraded_crusade
							any_war_enemy_country = {
								culture_group = giantkind
							}
							any_war_enemy_country = {
								culture_group = goblin
							}
						}
						any_war_enemy_country = {
							culture_group = dwarven
						}
					}
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = H83_dreamfire_crusade_at_war_with_dwarf
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = H83_dreamfire_crusade_at_war_with_dwarf }
				remove_country_modifier = H83_dreamfire_crusade_at_war_with_dwarf
			}
		}
	}
}

	# Charkuchin Kobold supplies for AI
	# Check if they can build a supply facility, and also give them a small boost
	# since they can't upgrade citadels and do other things the player can
	# We're aiming for the AI to have enough supply gain that they can "finish" the
	# system by having +527 supplies by around 1600
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = charkuchin_kobold_citadel_supplies_mechanic
			ai = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				treasury = 50
				NOT = {
					check_variable = {
						which = insyaa_charkuchin_kobold_citadel_supplies_supply_facility_count
						value = 10
					}
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					superregion = charkuchar_superregion # Only give them freebies in the mountain range
					is_city = yes
					NOT = {
						has_province_modifier = charkuchin_kobold_supply_facility
						has_charkuchin_kobold_citadel = yes
					}
				}
			}
			insyaa_charkuchin_kobolds_ai_supply_centre = yes
		}
		# Every 50 years, give the AI +150 monthly supplies 
		# Since this is inside a five year pulse, I need to make sure the window is five years
		# So, we start at 1444, next one is 1494-1498, then 1544-1548, then 1594-1598. They end up
		# with +450 monthly supplies which is what's needed to colonise the whole range
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_year = 1494
				NOT = { is_year = 1499 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = insyaa_charkuchin_kobold_citadel_supplies_total_gain
				value = 150
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_year = 1544
				NOT = { is_year = 1549 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = insyaa_charkuchin_kobold_citadel_supplies_total_gain
				value = 150
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_year = 1594
				NOT = { is_year = 1599 }
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = insyaa_charkuchin_kobold_citadel_supplies_total_gain
				value = 150
			}
		}
	}

	#Endhuvi Sarisung Rebels
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = R36 }
			sarisung_area = {
				has_province_modifier = R36_you_will_never_find_a_more_wretched_hive_mod

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_5 }
			remove_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_4 }
			remove_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_4
		}		
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_3 }
			remove_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_2 }
			remove_country_modifier = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_2
		}
		else_if = {

		else_if = {

				duration = 1825
			}

				duration = 1825
			}

				duration = 1825

				duration = 1825

				name = production_efficiency_from_strategic_goods_1
				duration = 1825

        limit = {
            tag = Z36
            is_subject_of = Z52
            capital_scope = {
                NOT = { province_group = hold_province }

            hold_province = { owned_by = Z36 }

        random_owned_province = {
           limit = { province_group = hold_province }
           ROOT = { set_capital = PREV }
        }
	}

		limit = {
			is_the_raja = yes
			ai = yes

			2 = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = rahen_raj_mandate_raja_4_raja_cd_mod }
					is_at_war = no
					calc_true_if = {
						all_subject_country = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_raj_wars } }
						amount = 8
					}
				}
				rahen_raj_mandate_raja_introspection = yes
				add_mil_power = -50
			}
			2 = {
				trigger = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = rahen_raj_mandate_raja_3_raja_mod } }
				rahen_raj_mandate_raja_declaration_of_harmony = yes
				add_dip_power = -50
			}
			2 = {
				trigger = {
					has_saved_global_event_target = raj_vizier_global_target
					event_target:raj_vizier_global_target = { ai = yes }
					NOT = { has_country_modifier = rahen_raj_mandate_vizier_2_raja_mod }
				}
				event_target:raj_vizier_global_target = {
					rahen_raj_mandate_vizier_imperial_drills = yes
					add_mil_power = -50
				}
			}
			13 = {}
		}
	}
}

on_death_has_harem = {
	if = { limit = { has_heir = no }
		if = { 
			limit = {
				eligble_for_harpy_harem_events = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = harpy_events.101 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_reform = namasonamingo_reform
			}
			country_event = { id = dakinshi_harem_events.2 }
		}
		else_if ={
			limit = {
				has_reform = ngwenamasonamingo_reform
			}
			country_event = { id = flavor_averilibet.2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_reform = kumarkand_emperor_rule
			}
			country_event = { id = flavor_kumarkand.105}
		}
	}
}

#1.35
on_province_religion_changed = { #Randomizer has fixed outcomes on this on action BEWARE
	on_province_religion_changed_effect = yes #1.35
	on_province_religion_converted_effect = yes #1.35 (Ignore this)

	###############################################################
	# EFFECTS BELOW HERE DO NOT WORK PROPERLY IN SCRIPTED EFFECTS #
	# most common causes are:                                     #
	# using a country event or similar in an else_if              #
	# or using a trigger switch                                   #
	###############################################################
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = suhans_praxis
			has_global_flag = suhan_goes_sicko_mode
			has_global_flag = suhan_4
			calc_true_if = {
				amount = 50
				rahen_superregion = {
					type = all
					NOT = { region = shamakhad_region }
					religion = suhans_praxis
				}
			}
		}
		owner = { country_event = { id = rahen.12 } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_saved_global_event_target = suhan_center
			has_global_flag = suhan_goes_sicko_mode
			has_global_flag = suhan_4
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:suhan_center = {
					NOT = { religion = suhans_praxis }
				}
			}
			event_target:suhan_center = {
				owner = {
					country_event = { id = rahen.11 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = L08_protected_minority
		}
		remove_province_modifier = L08_protected_minority
	}
	#Khugra
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = L70_enlightenment_by_force
			NOT = {
				religion = gods_of_the_taychend
				religion = oren_nayiru
				religion = oren_nayiru_reformed
				religion = gods_of_the_taychend_reformed
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = L70_enlightenment_by_force
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_government_mechanic = desert_legion_mechanic }
			has_province_modifier = jaddari_zealotry_darkness_province
		}
		remove_province_modifier = jaddari_zealotry_darkness_province
		if = {
			limit = {
				development = 25
			}
			owner = {
				add_government_power = { mechanic_type = desert_legion_mechanic power_type = jaddari_zealotry value = 6 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			owner = {
				add_government_power = { mechanic_type = desert_legion_mechanic power_type = jaddari_zealotry value = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	#Rakkaz
	if = {
		limit = { 
			religion = shadow_pact
			owner = { religion = shadow_pact } 
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = numOfProvincesConvertedToSP
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	#Brrtekuh
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = kvangahga
			owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_U10_followers_of_the_windstorm }
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = U10_serving_the_strongest duration = -1 }
	}
	
	#Raithtall
	if = {
		limit = { has_province_modifier = raithtall_disarmed_population }
		remove_province_modifier = raithtall_disarmed_population
	}
	#Shadow Pact Events
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = shadow_pact_purge_of_hags
			NOT = {
				religion = shadow_pact
				religion = night_coven
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = shadow_pact_purge_of_hags
	}
	#Zokka
	if = {
		limit = { has_province_modifier = zokka_left_behind }
		remove_province_modifier = zokka_left_behind
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { tag = F29 } }
		if = {
			limit = { religion = xhazobkult }
			zokka_xhazobkult_effect = yes
		}
		else = { zokka_religion_effect = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { religion_group = bulwari has_global_flag = zokka_killed_sun_cult_flag }
		remove_province_modifier = religious_zeal_at_conv
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = zokka_sunset_prov
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_province_modifier = zokka_sunset_prov NOT = { religion_group = bulwari } }
		remove_province_modifier = zokka_sunset_prov
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			F29 = { has_country_flag = zokka_sun_cult_tracker } 
			NOT = { continent = north_america } 
			NOT = { continent = south_america } 
			NOT = { continent = oceania } 
		}
		zokka_has_killed_sun_cult_yet_effect = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { #Events on temples converted to JAD
			religion = the_jadd
			owner = {
				religion = the_jadd
			}
			OR = {
				province_id = 643 #Azka Sur
				province_id = 631 #Eduz Vacyn
				province_id = 601 #Bulwar
			}
		}
		owner = {
			country_event = {
				id = bulwar_flavour.145
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bulwar_flavour.146
			}
			country_event = {
				id = bulwar_flavour.147
			}
		}
	} 
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = F66 }
				owns = 473
			}
			473 = {
				has_province_modifier = konolkhatep_high_temple_of_the_two
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = konolkhatep_high_temple_of_the_two_nirakhetist
		remove_province_modifier = konolkhatep_high_temple_of_the_two_elikhetist
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = nirakhetist
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = konolkhatep_high_temple_of_the_two_nirakhetist
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				religion = elikhetist
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = konolkhatep_high_temple_of_the_two_elikhetist
				duration = -1
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	#Accretive Path Events - Stones in the Stream
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = ap_stonesinstream_convert
			religion = accretive_path
		}
		province_event = {
			id = accretive_path_events.13
		}
	}

	#Yudunyovi
	if = {
		limit = { 
			religion = yudunyovi
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_personal_deity = yukel }
				NOT = { has_province_flag = had_ways_of_tranquily_mod }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = yudunyovi_ways_of_tranquility
				duration = 1825 #5 years
			}
			set_province_flag = had_ways_of_tranquily_mod
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_personal_deity = kalyin }
				NOT = { has_province_flag = had_sea_of_tranquily_mod }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = yudunyovi_sea_of_tranquility
				duration = 1825 #5 years
			}
			set_province_flag = had_sea_of_tranquily_mod
		}
	}
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = molten_eternity
			owner = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = volcanic_truth_zeal
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = 25
			}
		}
	}
	#Plateau Cultivation
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute  = plateau_cultivation } }
		# Add bonus/malus to Infinite Self provinces
		if = {
			limit = { religion = infinite_self }
			if = {
				limit = { province_with_arable_goods = yes }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gov_plateau_bonus
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { province_with_animal_goods = yes }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gov_plateau_malus
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
		# Remove modifiers if province converted away
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_province_modifier = gov_plateau_bonus
					has_province_modifier = gov_plateau_malus
				}
			}
			remove_province_modifier = gov_plateau_bonus
			remove_province_modifier = gov_plateau_malus
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			province_id = 6919
			has_global_flag = vt_convert_yahou_lapahtol_reward
			religion = volcanic_truth
		}
		remove_reform_center = molten_eternity
		add_reform_center = volcanic_truth
		oceania = {
			limit = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_province_modifier = religious_zeal_at_conv
			}
			remove_province_modifier = religious_zeal_at_conv
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = vt_molten_eternity_centre_converted
				duration = 7300 # 20 years
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = vt_convert_yahou_lapahtol_reward
	}
	#Beikling Culture changes
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				religion = devouring_path
				OR = {
					tag = V23 #Luzhong
					overlord = { tag = V23 } #Luzhong
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Yak Hobgoblin
			limit = {
				culture_group = hobgoblin
				owner = {
					OR = {
						accepted_culture = yak_command
						overlord = { accepted_culture = yak_command }
					}
				}
			}
			change_culture = yak_command
		}
		if = { #Hillsworn Harimari
			limit = {
				culture_group = harimari
				owner = {
					OR = {
						accepted_culture = hillsworn_harimari
						overlord = { accepted_culture = hillsworn_harimari }
					}
				}
			}
			change_culture = hillsworn_harimari
		}
		if = { #Nuraryi Harpy
			limit = {
				culture_group = harpy
				owner = {
					OR = {
						accepted_culture = nuraryi_harpy
						overlord = { accepted_culture = nuraryi_harpy  }
					}
				}
			}
			change_culture = nuraryi_harpy
		}
	}
}

	on_province_culture_converted_estate_privilges_effect = yes

	on_province_culture_converted_effect = yes
	# don't use this, it doesn't account for culture change by effect, use on_province_culture_changed
	if = { #This is here on purpose, it is only supposed to be activated on MANUAL culture conversion
		limit = {
			owner = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = B39 }
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = wyvernheart_cultural_events_timer }
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger = { owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = wyvernheart_401_recent } } }
				province_event = {
					id = flavour_wyvernheart.401
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = { owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = wyvernheart_402_recent } } }
				province_event = {
					id = flavour_wyvernheart.402
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = { owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = wyvernheart_403_recent } } }
				province_event = {
					id = flavour_wyvernheart.403
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = { owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = wyvernheart_404_recent } } }
				province_event = {
					id = flavour_wyvernheart.404
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	#The Red Citadel - Better Forging
	beikling_update_better_forging_effect = yes

	#karassk 
	#for province culture changing

		owner = {
			add_treasury = 10
		}
	}

	#shifter stuff for culture conversion
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = shifter_lodge_inactive
			OR = {
				culture = cyazizeta_lizardfolk
				culture_group = inyaswarosa
			}
			owner = {
				OR = {
					primary_culture = cyazizeta_lizardfolk
					culture_group = inyaswarosa
				}
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = shifter_lodge_inactive
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = shifter_lodge_hidden_shifter_amount
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = shifter_lodge_active
			duration = -1
			desc = shifter_fake_local_modifer_amount
		}
		owner = {
			shifter_lodge_bonus_increase = yes
		}
	}

	#shifter stuff for converting away
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = shifter_lodge_active
			NOT = {
				culture = cyazizeta_lizardfolk
				culture_group = inyaswarosa
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = shifter_lodge_hidden_shifter_amount
		remove_province_modifier = shifter_lodge_active
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = shifter_lodge_inactive
			duration = -1
		}
		owner = {
			shifter_lodge_bonus_decrease = yes
		}
	}

	#averilibet shifter stuff 
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_estate_privilege = estate_nobility_S53_tanizu_tradition_water
					has_estate_privilege = estate_nobility_S53_tanizu_tradition_covenant
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { culture = yeteferen }
			add_province_modifier = { name = shifters_generic_province_allow duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
		else = {
			remove_province_modifier = shifters_generic_province_allow
		}
	}

	if = { #Eighard
		limit = {
			superregion = ynn_superregion
            owner = {
                OR = {
                    mission_completed = H14_secure_fringes
                    AND = {
                        overlord = { mission_completed = H14_secure_fringes }
                        is_free_or_tributary_trigger = no
                    }
                }
            }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = ynnsman
					culture = steel_dwarf
					culture = horizon_elf
					culture = pipefoot_halfling
				}
			}

				name = H14_securing_fringes
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = H14_securing_fringes
			}
			remove_province_modifier = H14_securing_fringes
		}
	}
	if = { #Eighard
		limit = {
			owner = {
				mission_completed = H14_it_means_unity
			}
			culture = tuathak
		}
		owner = {
			add_manpower = 10
		}
	}

	#Ardimyan Minor (colonisers)
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = qeyikul_guryadaggan_autonomy
			NOT = { culture = guryadagga }
		}

	}
}

			#Several cases:
			# - Prevous owner is ai, new owner is ai or '---' (decolonised)
			#		-> Do nothing
			# - Prevous owner is player, new owner is ai or '---' (decolonised)
			#		-> Abort exploration for previous owner (player)
			# TODO: Add more

			if = {
				limit = { aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_this_province_trigger = { who = FROM } }
				aPUI_clear_all_province_exploration_flags = yes
				save_event_target_as = gene_pillar_exploration_province
				FROM = {
					gene_pillar_abandon_expedition_effect = { country_notification_event = yes }
					aPUI_clear_all_country_exploration_flags = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		#Re-setup the province
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_interaction_setup_done } }
			province_event = { id = gene_pillars.94 }
		}

	}
}

#province 1.35
on_parliament_seat_lost = {
	on_parliament_seat_lost_effect = yes

	remove_province_modifier = hold_has_parliament
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = H35
					was_tag = H35
				}
			}
			has_province_modifier = h35_building_from_parliament
		}
		remove_province_modifier = h35_building_from_parliament
	}
	#vaengheim parliament system
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				tag = Z88
			}
			OR = {
				has_province_modifier = Z88_harpy_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_east_dalr_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_troll_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_west_dalr_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_tarik_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_gray_orc_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_skamvin_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_reachman_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_olavish_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_gnome_seat
				has_province_modifier = Z88_kobold_seat
			}
		}
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_harpy_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_east_dalr_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_troll_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_west_dalr_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_tarik_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_gray_orc_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_skamvin_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_reachman_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_olavish_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_gnome_seat
		remove_province_modifier = Z88_kobold_seat
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = Z88_current_bonus_seats
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_reform = imperial_diversity }
			has_province_modifier = imperial_diversity_province_mod
		}
		remove_province_modifier = imperial_diversity_province_mod
	}
}

# province
on_consecrate_patriarch = {
	if = { #1.35
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = has_improved_consecration }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = consecrated_ground
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = rakkaz_local_cult_gives_manpower } }
		every_province_in_state = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_moment_of_congruence } NOT = { has_province_flag = zokka_congruence_flag } }
		every_province_in_state = {
			add_base_tax = 1
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = zokka_congruence_moment
				duration = -1
			}
			set_province_flag = zokka_congruence_flag
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_eternal_congruence } }
		every_province_in_state = {
			add_nationalism = -5
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { culture = sandfang_gnoll } NOT = { culture = primal_harimari } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = zokka_congruence
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# country. from = overlord
# The base scope of the on_action is the overlord, with no direct way of scoping to the subject triggering the on_action. You need to use every_subject_country.
on_accept_tribute = {
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = molten_eternity
			has_personal_deity = volcanic_truth_persistence
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moltenEternityObligationVar
			value = 75
		}
	}
	#Star Rider
	if = {
		limit = { 
			FROM = { has_country_flag = I69_magical_feudalism } 
		} 
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { at_least_magical_infrastructure_level_3 = yes }
				#Nothing
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magical_infrastructure_level_2 = yes }
				increase_magic_experience = { unmodified_amount = 0.5 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magical_infrastructure_level_1 = yes }
				increase_magic_experience = { unmodified_amount = 1 }
			}
			else = {
				increase_magic_experience = { unmodified_amount = 2 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = flavour_star_rider.11
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = I69_cooldown
				duration = 60
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# country. from = overlord
on_refuse_tribute = {
}

# country
on_leader_recruited = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_command_of_the_military
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			influence = 5
			duration = 3650
			desc = EST_VAL_NOBLE_LEADER
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_ajgriijarul_military_command
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_ajgriijarul
			influence = 5
			duration = 3650
			desc = EST_VAL_AJGRIIJARUL_LEADER
		}
	}
	if = { #1.35
		limit = { has_government_attribute = theocratic_monarchy_mechanic }
		change_statists_vs_orangists = 0.01
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_six_schools }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = all
			loyalty = 2
		}
		command_recruit_second_general_effect = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_isagumze_kulugi_abe_generals
		}
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			influence = 1
			duration = 3650
			desc = EST_VAL_NOBLE_LEADER
		}
	}

	if = { #Magic Rework
		limit = { has_country_modifier = orb_of_omniscience_leader_tracker }
		change_variable = { orb_of_omniscience_progress_tracker = 1 }
	}

	dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = iehu amount = 1 }

		#Submod: apply increased naval maintenance for being over naval FL
	if = {
		limit = {
			ai = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				naval_forcelimit = 1
			}
			# Remove existing modifier, if applicable
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_1
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_2
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_3
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_4
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_5
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_6
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_6
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_7
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_7
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_8
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_8
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_9
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_9
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_10
				}
				remove_country_modifier = sloots_over_naval_fl_10
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { 
					naval_forcelimit = 100
				}
				
				# Apply new modifier
				if = {
					limit = {
						navy_size_percentage = 3.5
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = sloots_over_naval_fl_10
						duration = -1
						desc = sloots_over_naval_fl_10_desc
					}
					
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						navy_size_percentage = 3.25
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = sloots_over_naval_fl_9
						duration = -1
						desc = sloots_over_naval_fl_9_desc
					}
					
				}

						name = sloots_over_naval_fl_4
						duration = -1
						desc = sloots_over_naval_fl_4_desc
					}
					
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						navy_size_percentage = 2.125
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = sloots_over_naval_fl_3
						duration = -1
						desc = sloots_over_naval_fl_3_desc
					}
					
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						navy_size_percentage = 1.75
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = sloots_over_naval_fl_2
						duration = -1
						desc = sloots_over_naval_fl_2_desc
					}
					
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						navy_size_percentage = 1.375
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = sloots_over_naval_fl_1
						duration = -1
						desc = sloots_over_naval_fl_1_desc
					}
					
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# country
on_admiral_recruited = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = admirals_give_army_professionalism }
		add_army_professionalism = 0.005
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = pol_global_maritime_empire_modifier
				has_country_modifier = pol_global_maritime_empire_2_modifier
			}
		}
		add_navy_tradition = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = improve_nav_prof_flag
		}
		add_navy_tradition = 1
	}
	#Anbennar
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = L62_admirals_increase_professionalism }
		add_army_professionalism = 0.01
	}
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = molten_eternity
			has_personal_deity = infinite_self_enrichment
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moltenEternityObligationVar
			value = 50
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_saved_global_event_target = grasswhirlpool }
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:grasswhirlpool = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					has_great_project = {
						type = grasswhirlpool
						tier = 2
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:grasswhirlpool = {
						has_great_project = {
							type = grasswhirlpool
							tier = 3
						}
					}
				}
				add_sailors = -500
			}
			else = {
				add_sailors = -250
			}
		}
	}
}

# THIS = Province, FROM = Country
on_regiment_recruited = {
	FROM = { #Anbennar
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_lion_command_war_room_rights }
			add_legitimacy = 0.2
		}
	}
	if = { #AI builds warrior-monks if it can
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_global_modifier_value = {
					which = has_samurai
					value = 1
				}
				ai = yes
				current_income_balance = 0.2
			}
			has_local_modifier_value = {
				which = local_has_samurai
				value = 1
			}
			infantry_in_province = FROM
		}
		FROM = { #This could be a variable arithmetic trigger
			export_to_variable = { #this is how many warrior-monks we currently have
				which = num_of_samurai_var
				value = trigger_value:num_of_samurai
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = {
						which = allowed_samurai_var
						which = num_of_samurai_var
					}
				}
			}
			province_event = { id = one_xia.3003 } #In an event to prevent CTDs
		}
	}
	FROM = { accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = sages_of_the_misty_mountains category = mil amount = 5 } }

	#Fangaulan Pantheon
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = fangaulan_pantheon
			}
			add_church_power = 0.1
		}
	}
}

# THIS = One province in the state
on_remove_pasha = {
	hidden_effect = {
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = province_owner
		}
		remove_province_modifier = pasha_removed_modifier
	}

	area = {
		limit = { owned_by = event_target:province_owner }
		add_or_extend_province_modifier_effect = { MODIFIER = pasha_removed_modifier DURATION = 3650 }

		if = { #1.35
			limit = { has_province_modifier = the_provincial_system }
			remove_province_modifier = the_provincial_system
		}
	}
}

			}
		} 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					owner = { has_country_flag = landslide_infantry_half_devastation }
					AND = { owner = { has_church_aspect = endless_ocean_landslide_wavesong_instructors } has_port = yes }
				}
			}
			add_devastation = 5 #Half Devastation
		} 
		else = { add_devastation = 10 } #Full Devastation
	}
	add_province_modifier = { #Allows Hazard Events to target province for 20 years
		name = landslide_infantry_hazards_possible
		duration = 7300
		hidden = yes
	}
	owner = {
		if = { #For grant_noble_flamesong_rights reform
			limit = { has_government_attribute = landslide_infantry_nobility_influence } 
			add_country_modifier = { name = yanacotle_noble_flamesong_rights_recruited duration = 1800 }
		}
	}

on_reform_enacted = {
	if = {
		limit = { religion = corinite }
		add_karma = 10
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = I89
			NOT = { has_country_flag = centaur_no_zeal }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = verdant_bliss_flag }
			add_faction = verdant_bliss
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = burning_spear_flag }
			add_faction = burning_spear
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = tiger_bane_flag }
			add_faction = tiger_bane
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = raging_blizzard_flag }
			add_faction = raging_blizzard
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = vine_tearer_flag }
			add_faction = vine_tearer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rosen_rider_flag }
			add_faction = rosen_rider
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_reform = bulwari_temple_reform
		}
		add_government_power = { mechanic_type = vacyntassi_temple_authority power_type = vacytassi_temple_authority_power value = 40 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = united_federation }
		kalsyto_faction_clear = yes
	}
	update_artifice_points = yes

	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = salla_cenag_yfel_cenag }
		add_or_extend_country_modifier = {
			name = salla_cenag_embrace_change
			duration = 1825
		}
	}

	#Tribal Chendhyans
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_1
				has_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_2
				has_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_3
				has_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_4
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_4
		remove_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_3
		remove_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_2
		remove_country_modifier = chendhya_ramping_up_1
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = reform_level
			5 = { 
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = chendhya_ramping_up_5
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			4 = { 
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = chendhya_ramping_up_4
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			3 = { 
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = chendhya_ramping_up_3
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			2 = { 
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = chendhya_ramping_up_2
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			1 = { 
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = chendhya_ramping_up_1
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	if = { #Centaur Nomadism/NZoC
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = has_centaur_nomadism_attribute
			NOT = { has_government_attribute = centaur_nomadism_attribute }
		}
		remove_centaur_nomadism = yes
	}
	if = { #Bonecarver
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = B27_reform_centre
			is_tribal = no
		}
		capital_scope = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						religion = great_dookan
					}
				}
				add_reform_center = great_dookan
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						religion = bulgu_orazan
					}
				}
				add_reform_center = bulgu_orazan
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = B27_reform_centre
	}
	if = { #Dragon turtles
		limit = {
			dragon_turtle_beloved = { dragon_turtle = naauao }
			has_government_attribute = heir
		}
		remove_country_modifier = naauao_no_heir_adm
		remove_country_modifier = naauao_no_heir_dip
		remove_country_modifier = naauao_no_heir_mil
	}
}

on_trade_company_investment = {
}

on_center_of_trade_upgrade = {
	events = {
		flavour_gor_vazumbrog.208
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = enable_upgrading_centers_of_trade_dev } }
		add_base_production = 1
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = geo_centers_of_trade } }
		add_base_production = 1 
	}

	#Pashaine
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = {
				OR = { 
					has_country_modifier = pashaine_closed_markets 
					has_country_modifier = pashaine_businori_trade_expertise 
				}
			}
		}
		add_base_production = 1
	}

	#Accretive Path
	owner = { accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = river_flows_in_you category = dip amount = 25 } }

	#Fangaulan Pantheon
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = fangaulan_pantheon
			}
			add_church_power = 3
		}
	}
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3
			owner = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = infinite_self_enrichment
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = 400
			}
		}
	}
	#Bazaar upgrade Level 3 CoT...
	if = {
		limit = {
			province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3
			continent = africa
			owner = {
				owns = 6592
				6592 = {
					has_great_project = {
						type = bazaar_of_100001_pearls
						tier = 2
					}
					can_use_bazaar_of_100001_pearls = yes
				}
				
			}
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			which = origin_culture
			value = culture
		}

		change_culture = owner
		set_province_flag = bazaar_upgraded_center
	}
	# Landshark
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_government_attribute = adoptive_kartel_clans_reform_effect } 
		}
		if = {
			limit = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			owner = { change_government_reform_progress = 20 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2 }
			owner = { change_government_reform_progress = 10 }
		}
	}
}

on_center_of_trade_downgrade = {
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = enable_upgrading_centers_of_trade_dev } }
		add_base_production = -1
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = geo_centers_of_trade } }
		add_base_production = -1 
	}

	#Fangaulan Pantheon
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				religion = fangaulan_pantheon
			}
		}
		owner = { add_church_power = -3 }
	}
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2
			owner = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = infinite_self_enrichment
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = -400
			}
		}
	}
	#when downgrade CoT which upgraded with monument effect.
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = bazaar_upgraded_center
		}
		clr_province_flag = bazaar_upgraded_center
		change_culture = variable:origin_culture
	}
}

on_culture_promoted = {
	on_culture_promoted_estate_privileges_effect = yes

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { accepted_culture = masnsih }
				has_country_flag = sands_cult_unlocked
			}
			clr_country_flag = sands_cult_unlocked
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { accepted_culture = brasanni }
				has_country_flag = seaway_cult_unlocked
			}
			clr_country_flag = seaway_cult_unlocked
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { accepted_culture = kuzarami }
				has_country_flag = moon_cult_unlocked
			}
			clr_country_flag = moon_cult_unlocked
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { accepted_culture = surani }
				has_country_flag = hammuraway_cult_unlocked
			}
			clr_country_flag = hammuraway_cult_unlocked
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { accepted_culture = sadnatu }
				has_country_flag = whitestone_cult_unlocked
			}
			clr_country_flag = whitestone_cult_unlocked
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = koroshesh_kheteratan_cultures_modifier
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = hapremiti
					accepted_culture = irsmahapan
					accepted_culture = asbaiwix
					accepted_culture = korosheshi
					accepted_culture = tijarikheti
					accepted_culture = horakheti
				}
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = koroshesh_kheteratan_cultures_modifier
		remove_accepted_culture = hapremiti
		remove_accepted_culture = irsmahapan
		remove_accepted_culture = asbaiwix
		remove_accepted_culture = korosheshi
		remove_accepted_culture = tijarikheti
		remove_accepted_culture = horakheti
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = vt_mechanim_cultural_impact
			has_mechanim_accepted_culture = no
		}
		remove_country_modifier = vt_mechanim_cultural_impact
	}
	accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = relive_past_lives category = dip amount = -50 }
	if = { #Ayarallen
		limit = {
			tag = F27
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = F27_goblin_tolerance
				NOT = {
					accepted_culture = exodus_goblin
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = F27_goblin_tolerance
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = F27_bulwari_tolerance
				OR = {
					NOT = { accepted_culture = bahari }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = gelkar }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = brasanni }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = surani }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = zanite }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = maqeti }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = masnsih }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = sadnatu }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = kuzarami }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = bulwari_half_elf }
					NOT = { accepted_culture = sun_elf }
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = F27_bulwari_tolerance
			remove_accepted_culture = bahari
			remove_accepted_culture = gelkar
			remove_accepted_culture = brasanni
			remove_accepted_culture = surani
			remove_accepted_culture = zanite
			remove_accepted_culture = maqeti
			remove_accepted_culture = masnsih
			remove_accepted_culture = sadnatu
			remove_accepted_culture = kuzarami
			remove_accepted_culture = bulwari_half_elf
			remove_accepted_culture = sun_elf
		}
	}

	#Bibyobi
	if = {
		limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = S98 } }
		S98_remove_culture_modifiers_effect = yes
	}
}

	}

	# using a country event or similar in an else_if              #

	###############################################################

	#shifter lodge activation/deactivation 
	if = {

			add_country_modifier = {
				name = shifter_make_state_button_work_without_cav
				duration = -1 
				hidden = yes
			}
		}

				duration = -1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = shifter_lodge_active
			remove_province_modifier = shifter_lodge_hidden_shifter_amount
		}
	}

	if = {

			owns = 6648
			religion = beast_memory
			OR = {
				culture_group = inyaswarosa
				accepted_culture = antmvura
			}

					tier = 2
				}

			}

		if = {
			limit = {

					has_great_project = {

						tier = 3
					}

# ROOT = Overlord, FROM = Minor
on_dependency_gained = {
	# if = {
	# 	limit = {
	# 		FROM = {
	# 			has_government_attribute = has_dutch_election
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# 	ROOT = {
	# 		country_event = {
	# 			id = dutch_republic.31
	# 		}# States General falls under a PU
	# 	}
	# }

	#Anbennar
	##############################################################################################
	#If you are adding an action here to automatically flip new vassals to a custom subject type,
	#or grant independence, or anything that modifies the vassal state
	#It must be done in an event (to enforce it runs last), or the game can crash (from a race condition)
	##############################################################################################
	
	if = { #Disable mandate if steward is vassalized
		limit = { FROM = { is_emperor_of_china = yes } }
		dismantle_empire_of_china = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				exists = L28
				L28 = { is_subject_of_type = commercial_enterprise }
			}
			L28 = { country_event = { id = khet_mandate.203 } }
		}
	}

	if = { #Turning new subjects into Prabhia for the Raja
		limit = {
			ROOT = { has_government_attribute = is_raja }						# Overlord must be the Raja
			FROM = {
				NOT = { has_reform = oracular_order_reform } 		# Tughayasa has their own thing.
				NOT = { is_subject_of_type = great_daimyo_vassal }	# Do nothing if already correct type.
				NOT = { is_subject_of_type = daimyo_vassal }		# Do nothing if already correct type.
				NOT = { is_subject_of_type = vizier_vassal }		# Do nothing if already correct type.
				NOT = { is_colonial_nation = yes }                  # Colonial Nations should not become Prabhi, as funny as it is
			}
		}
		# logic moved into event to prevent crashes
		FROM = { country_event = { id = rahenraj.5000 } }
	}

	if = { #Releasing Iosahars if vassalized
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_country_modifier = ynn_diplo is_subject_of_type = vassal num_of_subjects = 1 }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = ynn_events.316 } }
	}

	#convert tributaries to satrapies
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { is_emperor_of_china = yes }
			FROM = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state_anb }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = khet_mandate.02 } }
	}

	#convert satrapies to tributaries
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { is_emperor_of_china = no }
			FROM = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = khet_mandate.03 } }
	}

	#convert koroshesh league to vassal
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { tag = L28 is_subject_of_type = commercial_enterprise  }
			ROOT = { NOT = { has_country_flag = koroshesh_league_enabled } }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = khet_mandate.07 } }
	}
	
	#if new satrapy has tributaries, release them
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { is_emperor_of_china = yes }
			FROM = {
				is_subject_of_type = tributary_state
				has_subject_of_type = tributary_state_anb
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = khet_mandate.09 } }
	}

	
	FROM = { update_nsc_level_secondary_effects = yes }

	if = { #Turning vassals into Xiakens when you release or gain new vassals
		limit = {
			ROOT = { has_reform = wulin }
			FROM = { NOT = { has_reform = xiaken is_subject_of_type = tributary_state_anb } }
		}
		# logic moved into event to prevent crashes
		FROM = { country_event = { id = one_xia.3000 } }
	}

	if = { #Turning patronates into vassals if overlord not VO. 
		limit = {
			NOT = { tag = Y63 } # new overlord is not VO
			FROM = { is_subject_of_type = patronate }
		}
		# logic moved into event to prevent crashes
		FROM = { country_event = { id = verkalozovar_events.9999 } }
	}
	
	#Dhugajir-Nadimraj subject
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { tag = R72 } # Dhugajir
			FROM = { tag = R73 } # Nadimraj
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = ghavaanaj_lord_of_the_nadimraj
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	
	#Dhenijanraj events
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { mission_completed = R51_peridot_king }
			FROM = { tag = I18 }
		}
		ROOT = { country_event = { id = flavor_dhenijanraj.300 } }
		add_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = dhenijanraj_peridot_opinion_modifier
		}
		reverse_add_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = dhenijanraj_peridot_opinion_modifier
		}
	}

	country_event = { id = ynn_events.21 }  #Transfer Iosahar of Iosahar to the top overlord
	
	# Verkal Ozovar
	if = {
		limit = { ROOT = { tag = Y63 } }
		FROM = { unban_magic = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_grand_rune_amekh }
			FROM = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = Y63_grand_rune_amekh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_grand_rune_jolkin }
			FROM = {
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = Y63_grand_rune_jolkin
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#Command Slave States subject
	if = {
		limit = { ROOT = { tag = R62 } } # The Command
		FROM = {
			ban_magic = yes
			if = { # logic moved into event to prevent crashes
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							tag = R81
							is_subject_of_type = autonomous_vassal
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = the_command.3000 }
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { is_subject_of_type = slave_state }
			NOT = { culture_group = hobgoblin } #the command, and the revolter commands, fail here - so they don't get their slave states taken away by firing the event
			NOT = { has_country_flag = can_have_slave_states } #zokka fails here, as they can have slave states
			# everyone else passes and gets their slave states taken away
		}
		# logic moved into event to prevent crashes
		FROM = { country_event = { id = the_command.3001 } }
	}

	# Anbennar CNs gotta follow overlord culture for races. Religion is a bonus.
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				is_colonial_nation = yes
				NOT = { overlord = { tag = G52 } } #Ameion
			}
			export_to_variable  = { variable_name = majorityCulture value = dominant_culture }
			export_to_variable  = { variable_name = overlordCulture value = primary_culture who = ROOT } 
			export_to_variable  = { variable_name = overlordReligion value = religion who = ROOT } 
	
			# only change stuff if culture is different
			if = { limit = { NOT = { is_variable_equal = { which = majorityCulture which = overlordCulture } } }
				change_primary_culture = variable:overlordCulture	# use overlord race
				change_religion = variable:overlordReligion			# use overlord religion
				add_accepted_culture = variable:majorityCulture 	# we accept the majority natives.
			}
			capital_scope = {  # capital uses overlord culture and religion.
				change_culture = FROM
				change_religion = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	

	if = { #Makes vassals of ynnic overlords into iosahar
		limit = {
			overlord = {
				has_country_modifier = ynn_diplo
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ynn_events.990
			}
		}
	}

	# Racial Tolerance Setup
	FROM = {
		country_event = { id = race_setup_events.1 }		#Sets up Racial Tolerance Level
		country_event = { id = race_setup_events.2 }		#Ai only event for preferred tolerace
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				OR = {
					tag = G46 
					tag = H22
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = G55
					tag = U27
				}
				has_country_flag = G55_call_in_degakheion_flag
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = G55_degakheioni_funding
				duration = -1
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = G55_degakheioni_merchant_influence
				duration = -1
			}
		}

	FROM = { #Disable election for republic pu

				set_country_flag = was_republic_twin_empire
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { mission_completed = F98_good_measure }
		FROM = { add_country_modifier = { name = F98_song_and_steel duration = -1 } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = F98 FROM = { owns = 3020 } }
		country_event = { id = flavour_harpylen.15 }
	}
}
