# ROOT = New vassal, FROM = Overlord
on_create_vassal = {
	on_religion_change_estate_privileges_effect = yes

	#Anbennar	
	if = {
		limit = {
			monstrous_culture = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = no_longer_monstrous }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = monstrous_nation duration = -1 }
	}
	if = { limit = { capital_scope = { continent = serpentspine } }
		add_country_modifier = { name = reclaiming_dwarovar duration = -1 }
	}

	# For countries that have ended up outside the proper range of isolationism values
	if = {
		limit = {
			uses_isolationism = yes
		}
		check_isolation_level = yes
	}

	#country_event = { id = monstrous.100 days = 1 }
	#country_event = { id = anbennar_setup.9 }              # Sets up racial admin/mil
	#country_event = { id = race_setup_events.1 }           # Sets up Racial Tolerance Level
	#country_event = { id = race_setup_events.2 }           # Ai only event for preferred tolerace
	#country_event = { id = race_setup_events.19 }
	# unnecessary due to race_setup_events.22

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
		country_event = { id = race_setup_events.16 }
		country_event = { id = race_setup_events.19 } # recalculate tolerances
		# edge case - update majorities for vassals released on day 1 before the startup event was done
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			FROM = {
				is_revolutionary = yes
			}
		}
		change_government = republic
		add_government_reform = junior_revolutionary_republic_reform
		set_country_flag = had_revolution
	}
	if = { # Anbennar: changed to ravelian rectorate, our papacy
		limit = {
			tag = Z97
		}
		change_government = theocracy
		change_religion = ravelian
		add_government_reform = papacy_reform
		adopt_reform_progress = FROM
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
		set_country_flag = released_in_1444
	}

	country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.11 days = 1 }

	if = { #Makes vassals of ynnic overlords into iosahar
		limit = {
			overlord = {
				has_country_modifier = ynn_diplo
			}
		}
		release_iosahar = yes
		FROM = {
			create_iosahar = { tag = ROOT }
		}
	}
	
	# Verkal Ozovar
	if = {
		limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_grand_rune_amekh }
		FROM = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Y63_grand_rune_amekh
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_grand_rune_jolkin }
		FROM = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = Y63_grand_rune_jolkin
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { tag = H66 } #Jaherian Exemplars
			NOT = { tag = H67 } #Rezankand
			OR = {
				religion_group = bulwari
				has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window
			}
			government = theocracy
			ai = yes
		}
		add_government_reform = bulwari_temple_reform
		add_government_power = { mechanic_type = vacyntassi_temple_authority power_type = vacytassi_temple_authority_power value = 40 }
	}

	country_event = { id = eordellon.5 }

	if = {
		limit = { religion = kheionism }
		initialize_kheionism_variables = yes
		country_event = { id = kheionism.3 } #Set your deity
	}

	if = { #Shuvuush/Kuuldaar tags become horde and gets the privilege
		limit = {
			technology_group = tech_shuvuush
			NOT = {
				tag = Y98 #Daxugo
				tag = Y86 #Guwaamud
			}
		}
		change_government = tribal
		add_government_reform = steppe_horde
		country_event = { id = shuvuush.1000 days = 1 } #Adding the privilege, doesn't work within the same day/effect, need to delay with effect
	}

	#Charkuchin kobolds need their Supplies mechanic
	if = {
		limit = {
			charkuchin_kobold_culture = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				# This flag means the range has been united and the supplies mechanic done
				# In that case, don't turn it back on if a new country is released
				NOT = { has_global_flag = charkuchin_kobold_supplies_finished }
			}
			insyaa_charkuchin_kobolds_released_setup = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = charkuchin_kobold_supplies_finished_country #This flag is to replace supply with other stuff
		}
	}
}

# ROOT = Country establishing it
# FROM = Capital province of the area - the first one listed in the area definition in map\area.txt
# First province in state is set
on_holy_order_established = {
	ROOT = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = spiked_log_jadd_holy_order_refund_adm
			}
			clr_country_flag = spiked_log_jadd_holy_order_refund_adm
			add_adm_power = 25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = spiked_log_jadd_holy_order_refund_dip
			}
			clr_country_flag = spiked_log_jadd_holy_order_refund_dip
			add_dip_power = 25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = spiked_log_jadd_holy_order_refund_mil
			}
			clr_country_flag = spiked_log_jadd_holy_order_refund_mil
			add_mil_power = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_table_war }
			}
			owner = { add_manpower = 2.5 }
		}
	}
	# Having these effects here for Volcanic Truth prevents the error log spam from the tooltip
	# Plus it saves repeating the code 3 times in the 3 per_province_effect clauses
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					holy_order = tlanhau_order
					holy_order = molomoa_order
					holy_order = cuauholoi_order
				}
				region = tagaala_mangroves_region
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = vt_taga_ala_trade_dip_order
					NOT = { has_province_flag = vt_taga_ala_trade_active_province }
				}
				area = {
					add_permanent_province_modifier = {
						name = vt_taga_ala_province_dip_order_trade_modifier
						duration = 730
					}
					set_province_flag = vt_taga_ala_trade_active_province
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = vt_taga_ala_convert_dip_order
					NOT = { has_province_flag = vt_taga_ala_convert_active_province }
				}
				area = {
					add_base_production = 1
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { religion = volcanic_truth }
						}
						random = {
							chance = 25
							change_religion = volcanic_truth
						}
					}
					set_province_flag = vt_taga_ala_convert_active_province
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = vt_taga_ala_war_dip_order
				}
				area = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { religion = volcanic_truth }
						}
						add_devastation = 50
						change_religion = volcanic_truth
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Landslide Infantry
			limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_church_landslide_inquisitors } }
			area = {
				limit = { has_owner_religion = no }
				add_province_modifier = { name = yanacotle_landslide_inquisitors duration = 3600 }
			}
		}
	}
	ROOT = { # Trust me, you need this ROOT
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = volcanic_truth
				has_global_flag = vt_taga_ala_war_dip_order
				FROM = { region = tagaala_mangroves_region }
			}
			if = { #Once you've conquered the whole Taga'ala region and assigned a Holy Order, you get the reward
				limit = {
					tagaala_mangroves_region = {
						type = all
						owned_by = ROOT
						has_volcanic_truth_holy_order_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = volcanic_truth.201
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Explainer event
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = vt_war_on_taga_ala_total_conquest }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = volcanic_truth.200
				}
				set_country_flag = vt_war_on_taga_ala_total_conquest
			}
		}
	}
	ROOT = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = B42
					was_tag = B42
				}
				has_country_modifier = B42_free_order
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_province_flag = B42_set_free_order } 
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				set_province_flag = B42_set_free_order
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = B42_free_holy_order
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = B42_free_holy_order
							value = 1
						}						
					}

				}
				remove_country_modifier = B42_free_order
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = F80 } religion = bulwari_sun_cult mission_completed = F80_mission_our_duty }
			FROM = {
				area = { limit = { culture_group = harpy }
					owner = {
						if = { limit = { has_country_modifier = monstrous_nation }
							decrease_monstrous_1 = yes
						}
						else = {
							change_government_reform_progress = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# When a minority is expelled to a colony
# THIS = Colony, ROOT = Colony, FROM = Home province
on_minority_expelled = {
	FROM = {
		remove_province_modifier = religious_zeal_at_conv
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = expelled_minority_home
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
}

# THIS = Raiding country, FROM = Sea province
on_raid_coast = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_faction = pr_buccaneers
		}
		add_faction_influence = {
			faction = pr_buccaneers
			influence = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_government_attribute = raiding_increases_pp
				has_country_flag = RSP_the_king_of_the_pirates
			}
		}
		add_power_projection = {
			type = high_sea_power_projection
			amount = 1
		}
	}
	#Anbennar: we don't have this mission
	# if = {
		# limit = {
			# has_mission = dan_raid_the_north_sea
			# NOT = { mission_completed = dan_raid_the_north_sea }
		# }
		# change_variable = {
			# which = num_of_raided_coasts
			# value = 1
		# }
	# }

	#Anbennar
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = pirate_republic_shared_loot
			has_reform = pirate_republic_reform
		}
		add_republican_tradition = 0.25
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = kvangahga
		}
		add_church_power = 2.5
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = xhazobkult
		}
		add_patriarch_authority = 0.005
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = demonicPowerGained
				value = 0.5
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ruler_has_personality = xhazobs_chosen_personality }
				change_variable = {
					which = demonicPowerGainedByXhazobine
					value = 0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_reform = F66_eternal_empire
		}
		FROM = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = slaves_raided
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = konol_slave_raid_cooldown }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 10
					konolkhatep_slave_raid_effect = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_terrain = city_terrain
							has_terrain = dwarven_hold_surface
						}
					}
					F66 = { konolkhatep_add_slaves = { slaves = 4 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_terrain = farmlands
							has_terrain = grasslands
							has_terrain = drylands
							has_terrain = coastline
						}
					}
					F66 = { konolkhatep_add_slaves = { slaves = 3 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_terrain = savannah
							has_terrain = steppe
							has_terrain = forest
							has_terrain = bloodgroves
							has_terrain = hills
							has_terrain = woods
							has_terrain = jungle
							has_terrain = highlands
						}
					}
					F66 = { konolkhatep_add_slaves = { slaves = 2 } }
				}
				else = {
					F66 = { konolkhatep_add_slaves = { slaves = 1 } }
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = konol_slave_raid_cooldown
					duration = 3650
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Mykx
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = mykx_raid_gives_tributary_cb }
		FROM = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = slaves_raided
					owner = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = mykx_slave_raid_cb_duration } }
				}
				owner = {
					reverse_add_casus_belli = {
						target = ROOT
						type = cb_force_tributary_mission
						months = 120
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = mykx_slave_raid_cb_duration
						duration = 3650
						hidden = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Reveria
	if = { #Gov Reform
		limit = { has_reform = reaver_noble_class }
		add_splendor = 2
		add_navy_tradition = 1
	}
	if = { #The Though Final Reward
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = reveria_the_thought_final_reward
		}
		FROM = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_modifier = slaves_raided 
					development = 24
				}
				ROOT = {
					change_government_reform_progress = 20
					change_innovativeness = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = { #Cannorian Group Generic Reward
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = reveria_generic_final_reward
		}
		FROM = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = { 
					has_province_modifier = slaves_raided 
					NOT = { religion_group = cannorian }
				}
				ROOT = { 
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = reveria_cannorian_raid3 } }
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_modifier = reveria_cannorian_raid2 }
							remove_country_modifier = reveria_cannorian_raid2
							add_country_modifier = {
								name = reveria_cannorian_raid3
								duration = 1825
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = { has_country_modifier = reveria_cannorian_raid1 }
							remove_country_modifier = reveria_cannorian_raid1
							add_country_modifier = {
								name = reveria_cannorian_raid2
								duration = 1825
							}
						}
						else = {
							add_country_modifier = {
								name = reveria_cannorian_raid1
								duration = 1825
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						remove_country_modifier = reveria_cannorian_raid3
						add_country_modifier = {
							name = reveria_cannorian_raid3
							duration = 1825
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			1081 = { owned_by = ROOT }
		}
		FROM = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided }
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = {
						which = theDriftcourtTriggerVariable
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				1081 = { the_driftcourt_usage_trigger = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					1081 = {
						has_great_project = {
							type = the_driftcourt
							tier = 3
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					every_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided }
						add_claim = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					1081 = {
						has_great_project = {
							type = the_driftcourt
							tier = 1
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					every_neighbor_province = {
						limit = { 
							has_province_modifier = slaves_raided 
							OR = {
								continent = north_america
								continent = south_america
							}
						}
						add_claim = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Ruined Sea Pirates
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = RSP_treasure_hunt_system_enabled }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { which = RSPTreasureHunt value = 20 } }
			FROM = { random_neighbor_province = { limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided } set_province_flag = RSP_buried_treasure } }
			set_variable = { RSPTreasureHunt = 0 }
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				every_neighbor_province = { 
					limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided }
					ROOT = {
						change_variable = { which = RSPTreasureHunt value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = RSP_pillaging_the_shores_unlocked }
		if = {
			limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = J95 } }
			FROM = { every_neighbor_province = { limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided } ROOT = { add_army_professionalism = 0.00025 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = J96 } }
			FROM = { every_neighbor_province = { limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided } ROOT = { add_church_power = 0.25 } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = J97 } }
			FROM = { every_neighbor_province = { limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided } ROOT = { change_mana = { amount = 0.25 } } } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = J98 } }
			FROM = { every_neighbor_province = { limit = { has_province_modifier = slaves_raided } ROOT = { change_innovativeness = 0.025 } } }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = J97 }
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					any_neighbor_province = { 
						has_province_modifier = slaves_raided 
						trade_goods = precursor_relics 
					} 
				} 
			} 
			J97 = { set_country_flag = RSP_trollshaunt_raided_precursor_relics_province } 
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				FROM = { 
					any_neighbor_province = { 
						has_province_modifier = slaves_raided 
						trade_goods = damestear 
					} 
				} 
			} 
			J97 = { set_country_flag = RSP_trollshaunt_raided_damestear_province } 
		}
	}
}

# ROOT = Tag that captured the flagship, FROM = Tag that lost the flagship
# If using ROOT, explicitly scope to it, there may not be a default scope
on_flagship_captured = {
	FROM = {
		set_country_flag = captured_flagship_country_flag
	}
	ROOT = {
		country_event = { id = flagship_events.2 }
		set_country_flag = trophy_hunter_flag
	}
	FROM = {
		country_event = { id = flagship_events.1 }
	}
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = hsa_pride_eagle_of_the_fleet_modifier }
			remove_country_modifier = hsa_pride_eagle_of_the_fleet_modifier
		}
	}

	#Anbennar
	if = {
		limit = { ROOT = { is_subject_of_type = acolyte_dominion } }
		ROOT = {
			change_variable = { aInfluence = 5 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_subject_of_type = acolyte_dominion } }
		FROM = {
			subtract_variable = { aInfluence = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { aInfluence = 0 } } }
				set_variable = { aInfluence = 0 }
			}
		}
	}

	# Ovdal Tungr Sea Hold
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = F23_sea_hold_active
			}
			clr_country_flag = F23_sea_hold_active
			add_stability = -3
			# TODO OT, penalties for losing the Sea Hold.
		}
	}

}

# ROOT = Tag that destroyed the flagship, FROM = Tag that lost the flagship
# If using ROOT, explicitly scope to it, there is no default scope
on_flagship_destroyed = {
	FROM = {
		set_country_flag = sunk_flagship_country_flag
	}
	ROOT = {
		country_event = { id = flagship_events.4 }
	}
	FROM = {
		country_event = { id = flagship_events.3 }
	}
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = hsa_pride_eagle_of_the_fleet_modifier }
			remove_country_modifier = hsa_pride_eagle_of_the_fleet_modifier
		}
	}

	#Anbennar
	if = {
		limit = { ROOT = { is_subject_of_type = acolyte_dominion } }
		ROOT = {
			change_variable = { aInfluence = 5 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { is_subject_of_type = acolyte_dominion } }
		FROM = {
			subtract_variable = { aInfluence = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { aInfluence = 0 } } }
				set_variable = { aInfluence = 0 }
			}
		}
	}

	# Ovdal Tungr Sea Hold
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = F23_sea_hold_active
			}
			clr_country_flag = F23_sea_hold_active
			add_stability = -3
			# TODO OT, penalties for losing the Sea Hold.
		}
	}
}

# this = Released country, FROM = country sending the peace offer to force release
#NOTE: as of 1.36, only fires when releasing a nation via peace treaty and not via "release = <tag>" effect
on_country_released = {
	#Anbennar
	if = {
		limit = {
			monstrous_culture = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = no_longer_monstrous }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = monstrous_nation duration = -1 }
	}
	if = { limit = { capital_scope = { continent = serpentspine } }
		add_country_modifier = { name = reclaiming_dwarovar duration = -1 }
	}

	# For countries that have ended up outside the proper range of isolationism values
	if = {
		limit = {
			uses_isolationism = yes
		}
		check_isolation_level = yes
	}

	#country_event = { id = anbennar_setup.19 }
	#country_event = { id = anbennar_setup.9 }              # Sets up racial admin/mil
	#country_event = { id = race_setup_events.1 }           # Sets up Racial Tolerance Level
	#country_event = { id = race_setup_events.2 }           # Ai only event for preferred tolerace
	#country_event = { id = monstrous.100 days = 1 }
	# unnecessary due to race_setup_events.22

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
		country_event = { id = race_setup_events.16 }
		country_event = { id = race_setup_events.19 } # recalculate tolerances
		# edge case - update majorities for countries released on day 1 before the startup event was done
	}


	if = { # Anbennar: changed to ravelian rectorate, our papacy
		limit = {
			tag = Z97
		}
		change_government = theocracy
		change_religion = ravelian	#changed this from catholic
		add_government_reform = papacy_reform
		adopt_reform_progress = FROM
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_reform = religious_permanent_revolution_reform }
		}
		change_religion = FROM
		adopt_reform_progress = FROM
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = global_holy_war_released_modifier
			duration = 3650
			hidden = yes
		}
		capital_scope = {
			change_religion = FROM
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { is_year = 1445 } }
		set_country_flag = released_in_1444
	}

	
	if = {
		limit = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = xianjie_region
					area = rangadevi_area
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				has_reform = wulin
			}
		}
		add_government_reform = xiaken
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					region = xianjie_region
					area = rangadevi_area
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					tag = R62
					has_reform = wulin
				}
			}
		}
		add_government_reform = indep_xiaken
	}

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Emperor" } }
		if = {
			limit = { religion = ravelian }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = first_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = first_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = first_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = first_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = second_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = second_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = second_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = second_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = third_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = third_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = third_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = third_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = fourth_council_harsh }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = fourth_council_harsh
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = fourth_council_conciliatory }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = fourth_council_conciliatory
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ynnic_setup_effect = yes

	country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.11 days = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { tag = H66 } #Jaherian Exemplars
			NOT = { tag = H67 } #Rezankand 
			OR = {
				religion_group = bulwari
				has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window

			ai = yes
		}

		add_government_power = { mechanic_type = vacyntassi_temple_authority power_type = vacytassi_temple_authority_power value = 40 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				religion = corinite
				NOT = { has_country_flag = corinite_adm_order_picked }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = corinite.300
			days = 7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				religion = corinite
				NOT = { has_country_flag = corinite_dip_order_picked }
			}
		}

			id = corinite.301
			days = 7
		}
	}
	else_if = {

			AND = {
				religion = corinite
				NOT = { has_country_flag = corinite_mil_order_picked }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = corinite.302
			days = 7
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				religion = eordellon
				religion = spring_court
				religion = summer_court
				religion = autumn_court
				religion = winter_court
			}
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = seasonal_court_level_zero }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = seasonal_court_level_one }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = seasonal_court_level_two }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = seasonal_court_level_three }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = seasonal_court_level_four }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = eordellon.5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { religion = kheionism }
		initialize_kheionism_variables = yes
		country_event = { id = kheionism.3 } #Set your deity
	}

	# Samsumbat
	# If the country was released from the target of our special liberation CB, give them the special gov reform
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = F60 }
				has_country_flag = F60_custom_liberation_cb_target_country # This flag is set in the requestpeace pre_effect
			}
		}
		add_government_reform = republic_of_free_peoples
	}

	if = { #Shuvuush/Kuuldaar tags become horde and gets the privilege
		limit = {
			technology_group = tech_shuvuush
			NOT = {
				tag = Y98 #Daxugo
				tag = Y86 #Guwaamud
			}
		}
		change_government = tribal
		add_government_reform = steppe_horde
		country_event = { id = shuvuush.1000 days = 1 } #Adding the privilege, doesn't work within the same day/effect, need to delay with effect
	}
	if = { # istralore empire expanding
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = A45_liberation
			}
			capital_scope = {
				continent = europe
			}
		}
		set_in_empire = yes
	}

	#Fangaula Pantheon
	if = {
		limit = { religion = fangaulan_pantheon }
		fangaulan_pantheon_apply_holy_site_bonus = yes
	}

	#Charkuchin kobolds need their Supplies mechanic
	if = {
		limit = {
			charkuchin_kobold_culture = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				# This flag means the range has been united and the supplies mechanic done
				# In that case, don't turn it back on if a new country is released
				NOT = { has_global_flag = charkuchin_kobold_supplies_finished }
			}
			insyaa_charkuchin_kobolds_released_setup = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = charkuchin_kobold_supplies_finished_country #This flag is to replace supply with other stuff
		}
	}
}

# ROOT = province, FROM = country
on_trade_good_changed = {
	on_trade_good_changed_estate_privileges_effect = yes
	on_trade_good_changed_government_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { trade_goods = damestear }
		set_province_flag = has_damestear_flag
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_province_flag = has_damestear_flag }
		clr_province_flag = has_damestear_flag
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			has_province_modifier = big_fungi
			is_city = yes
			NOT = { trade_goods = fungi }
		}
		remove_province_modifier = big_fungi
	}
	
	remove_province_modifier = gold_hold
	if = {
		limit = { trade_goods = gold province_group = hold_province }
		add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = gold_hold duration = -1 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_multiracial_crop_rotation }
			OR = {
				trade_goods = fungi
				trade_goods = serpentbloom
				trade_goods = livestock
				trade_goods = grain
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					trade_goods = fungi
					trade_goods = serpentbloom
				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = skewered_drake_crop_caves duration = -1 hidden = yes }
		}
		else = { add_province_modifier = { name = skewered_drake_crop_other duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_G57_land_golden_ears }

					trade_goods = livestock

		remove_province_modifier = wine_bonus_prod
		remove_province_modifier = grain_bonus_prod
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_wine_ageifier
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_growth_beans
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_pearl_cultivators
		remove_province_modifier = wine_lord_wine
		remove_province_modifier = G58_sugar_province_goods
		remove_province_modifier = eordan_expedition_site
		remove_province_modifier = damestear_rich_deposit
		remove_province_modifier = huge_damestear

		remove_province_modifier = B34_board_of_chains_boost_upgraded
		remove_province_modifier = B34_board_of_chains_boost_upgraded_2
		remove_province_modifier = livestock_boost_frontier

		remove_province_modifier = J84_masquerade_relics
		remove_province_modifier = copperlord_copper

# this = country
on_loan_repaid = {
	on_loan_repaid_estate_privileges_effect = yes
	if = { #1.35 - Anbennar removed the THIS scope for causing errors
		limit = { 
			economic_ideas = 4 
		}
		add_inflation = -0.05
	}
	accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = teachings_of_balris category = adm amount = 10 }
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = molten_eternity
			has_personal_deity = infinite_self_enrichment
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moltenEternityObligationVar
			value = 3
		}
	}
	dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = kahuzaie amount = 1 }
}

# this = country 
on_rebels_break_country = {
	add_country_modifier = {
		name = just_lost_to_rebels
		duration = 10
		hidden = yes
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { is_subject_of_type = acolyte_dominion }
		divide_variable = { aInfluence = 2 }
	}
	
	if = { #Besolaki
		limit = { has_country_flag = G54_supporting_peasant_rebels_flag }
		if = {
			limit = { exists = U27 }
			U27 = { #Theinos
				country_event = {
					id = besolaki_events.50
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			G54 = { #Besolaki
				country_event = {
					id = besolaki_events.50
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = G54_supporting_peasant_rebels_flag
	}

	if = { #Larankar
		limit = { has_country_flag = G64_narathya_ruler_flag }
		set_country_flag = G64_sibling_died_early_flag
		country_event = {
			id = larankar_events.107 #Sibling's War Ends (Techeladar)
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = G64_tesheladar_ruler_flag }
		set_country_flag = G64_sibling_died_early_flag
		country_event = {
			id = larankar_events.106 #Sibling's War Ends (Narathya)
		}
	}

	events = {
		flavour_brelar.13		#boats revolt
		flavor_kalsyto.914		#Constitutional Crisis failure
		flavour_beggaston.2		# Freodam invasion
		effelai_worship.608 	#thavoii lost to rebels during onslaught
		effelai_worship.614		#parura lost to leechmen
	}

}

# this = country
## Fires when you fire or replace your ADM advisor, in the moment before they are actually removed from their post.
## Note: Defining a new advisor here will result in the shortest appointment in history. Use on_post_adm_advisor_fired instead :)
on_pre_adm_advisor_fired = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = need_to_fire_adm_advisor
		}
		set_country_flag = just_fired_adm_advisor
		remove_advisor_by_category_no_action = ADM
	}
	#remove advisor mods for pasiragha
	if = { 
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = pasiragha_flag_improved_philosophers
		}
		pasiragha_effect_clear_philosopher_mods = yes
	}
	#Rakkaz MT
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_organization_rule_of_warlocks
			NOT = { has_country_flag = in_rakkaz_warlock_event }
		}
		rakkaz_warlock_advisor_management = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { had_country_flag = { flag = adm_advisor_recently_hired days = 1825 } } }
		accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = acts_of_hermitage category = adm amount = -25 }
	}
	clr_country_flag = adm_advisor_recently_hired
	clr_country_flag = I55_adm_advisor_project_flag
	
	#Pachpalka
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = pachpalka_hired }
		pachpalka_fired_from_court_effect = { type = theologian }
		pachpalka_fired_from_court_effect = { type = artist }
		pachpalka_fired_from_court_effect = { type = philosopher }
	}

	# Parusahan Saya MT - Right-Hand Mage check
	if = {
		limit = { 
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = R54 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = R54_right_hand_mage
			}
			remove_country_modifier = R54_right_hand_mage
		}
	}
}

on_pre_dip_advisor_fired = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = need_to_fire_dip_advisor
		}
		set_country_flag = just_fired_dip_advisor
		remove_advisor_by_category_no_action = DIP
	}

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { had_country_flag = { flag = dip_advisor_recently_hired days = 1825 } } }
		accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = acts_of_hermitage category = adm amount = -25 }
	}
	clr_country_flag = dip_advisor_recently_hired
	clr_country_flag = I55_dip_advisor_project_flag
	clr_country_flag = Y15_dip_advisor_hired
	#Pachpalka
	pachpalka_fired_from_court_effect = { type = trader }
}

on_pre_mil_advisor_fired = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = need_to_fire_mil_advisor
		}
		set_country_flag = just_fired_mil_advisor
		remove_advisor_by_category_no_action = MIL

			has_country_modifier = az_an_two_shock_advisor
		}
		remove_country_modifier = az_an_two_shock_advisor
	}

	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { had_country_flag = { flag = mil_advisor_recently_hired days = 1825 } } }
		accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = acts_of_hermitage category = adm amount = -25 }
	}
	clr_country_flag = mil_advisor_recently_hired
	clr_country_flag = I55_mil_advisor_project_flag
}

# this = country
on_post_adm_advisor_fired = {
	on_advisor_removed_effct = { type = adm }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = rinta_path_merfolk_advisors
		}
		remove_country_modifier = merfolk_advisor_philosopher_modifier
	}

	#Ashhana Lizardfolk gain Canvas Control for advisors
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = ashhana_blood_curse_mechanic
		}
		remove_country_modifier = ashhana_control_adm_advisor
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = hyti_dreamer_employed } 
		country_event = { id = hyti.2 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 1 } }
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_artist_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_inquisitor_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_master_of_mint_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_natural_scientist_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_philosopher_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_theologian_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_treasurer_mod
	}
}

on_post_dip_advisor_fired = {
	on_advisor_removed_effct = { type = dip }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = rinta_path_merfolk_advisors
		}
		remove_country_modifier = merfolk_advisor_nreformer_modifier
		remove_country_modifier = merfolk_advisor_trader_modifier
	}

	if = { #Great Storm
		limit = { has_country_modifier = I80_big_cat_government }
		remove_country_modifier = I80_big_cat_government
	}


	#Ashhana Lizardfolk gain Canvas Control for advisors
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = ashhana_blood_curse_mechanic
		}
		remove_country_modifier = ashhana_control_dip_advisor
	}

	if = {
		limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 1 } }
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_colonial_governor_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_diplomat_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_naval_reformer_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_navigator_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_spymaster_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_statesman_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_trader_mod
	}
}

# this = country

	on_advisor_removed_effct = { type = mil }

	#Ashhana Lizardfolk gain Canvas Control for advisors
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = ashhana_blood_curse_mechanic
		}

	}

	if = {
		limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 1 } }
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_army_organiser_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_army_reformer_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_commandant_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_grand_captain_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_recruitmaster_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_fortification_expert_mod
		remove_country_modifier = divination_1_eye_for_talent_quartermaster_mod
	}
}

# this = new client state, from = parent country

	country_event = { id = racial_modifiers.6 days = 1 }	#Racial mil change if unmatching
	country_event = {
		id = anbennar_setup.19
	}
}

# this = new target, from = previous target (both can be non-existent tag)
on_change_revolution_target = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = junior_revolutionary_republic_reform }
		add_government_reform = revolutionary_republic_reform
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = pashaine_always_revolution_target
			ai = yes
			FROM = { 
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = B59 } #Pashaine
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		set_revolution_target = FROM
	}
}

# this = curia controller (enactor of the bull)
on_golden_bull_enacted = {
	set_country_flag = enacted_golden_bull
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = enacting_bull_1_stab_50_adm
		}
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
	}
}

on_country_creation = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = Z97
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					religion = ravelian
				}
				NOT = {
					has_reform = papacy_reform
				}
				NOT = {
					government = theocracy
				}
			}
		}
		change_religion = ravelian
		change_government = theocracy
		add_government_reform = papacy_reform
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_reform = adventurer_reform
				has_reform = dwarovar_warband
				has_reform = roaming_horde
			}
			ai = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { capital_scope = { continent = serpentspine } }
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = dont_colonize_but_migrate
				duration = 3650
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = dont_colonize_but_migrate
				duration = 365
				hidden = yes
			}
		}
	}
	country_event = {
		id = anbennar_setup.19
	}

	country_event = { id = new_sun_cult.11 days = 1 }

	if = { #Makes Beikdugang created subjects (mainly colonies) tolerate ruinborn more.
		limit = {
			overlord = { 
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = Y15 }
				mission_completed = Y15_solstice
			}
		}
		largest_increase_of_ruinborn_tolerance_effect = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { tag = H66 } #Jaherian Exemplars
			NOT = { tag = H67 } #Rezankand 
			OR = {
				religion_group = bulwari
				has_country_flag = updating_isolationism_window
			}
			government = theocracy
			ai = yes
		}
		add_government_reform = bulwari_temple_reform
		add_government_power = { mechanic_type = vacyntassi_temple_authority power_type = vacytassi_temple_authority_power value = 40 }
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = rending_active
			OR = {
				capital_scope = {
					continent = asia
					NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
				}
				num_of_owned_provinces_with = {
					value = 10
					continent = asia
					NOT = { superregion = forbidden_lands_superregion }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = accretive_path
					religion = transmutative_path
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = spirits.704 days = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = devouring_path
					religion = black_doctrine
				}
				
			}
			set_country_flag = rending_corrupt_flag
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = neokttareum
					religion = mystic_accord
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = rending_appease_flag
		}
		else = { set_country_flag = rending_ward_flag }
	}

	#Pick Holy Order
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				religion = corinite
				NOT = { has_country_flag = corinite_adm_order_picked }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = corinite.300
			days = 7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				religion = corinite
				NOT = { has_country_flag = corinite_dip_order_picked }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = corinite.301
			days = 7
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				religion = corinite
				NOT = { has_country_flag = corinite_mil_order_picked }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = corinite.302
			days = 7
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { religion = kheionism }
		initialize_kheionism_variables = yes
		country_event = { id = kheionism.3 } #Set your deity
	}

	#Fangaula Pantheon
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = fangaulan_pantheon
		}
		fangaulan_pantheon_apply_holy_site_bonus = yes
	}
}

# ROOT = country, FROM = country they fled from
on_cossacks_receive_serfs = {
}

on_federation_leader_change = {
	if = {
		limit = { tag = FROM }
		disband_federation = THIS
	}
	else = {
		# New strongest member becomes the new federation leader
		set_federation_leader = THIS
	}
}

#FROM = country pillaged, ROOT = country doing the pillaging
on_pillaged_capital = {
	slave_raid_pillage_capital_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					superregion = rahen_superregion
					superregion = yanshen_superregion
					superregion = vimdatrong_superregion
				}
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = rending_pillage_counter_variable
			value = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { religion = devouring_path }
		add_church_power = 50
	}
	if = {
		limit = { mission_completed = yuanszi_burn_heart }
		4559 = { add_or_extend_province_modifier_effect = { MODIFIER = yuanszi_fires_conviction DURATION = 1825 } }
	}
	#Dogeater
	if = {
		limit = {
			mission_completed = B28_i_have_an_announcement_to_make
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = B28_not_shown_off
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = B28_mockery
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_adm_power = 50
		add_mil_power = 50
		add_dip_power = 50
		add_treasury = 100
		add_war_exhaustion = -5
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { stability = -2 } }
			add_stability = 1
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
					name = orc_clans_contribution
					duration = 3650
		}
		FROM = {
			add_treasury = -100
			remove_opinion = {
				WHO = ROOT
				modifier = B28_mockery
			}
			reverse_remove_opinion = {
				WHO = ROOT
				modifier = B28_mockery
			}
			clr_country_flag = B28_not_shown_off
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = S90
				tag = S30
			}
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = S90_pillage_counter_variable
			value = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_reform = tsukqiao_throne_of_lies_reform }
		add_legitimacy = 5
	}
}

on_estate_led_regency = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = improved_nobles_regency
			OR = {
				has_estate = estate_nobles
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_estate = estate_nobles }
					# OR = {
					# 	has_estate = estate_maratha
					# 	has_estate = estate_rajput
						#Anbennar
						has_estate = estate_uppercastes
					# }
				}
			}
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = empowered_regency_modifier
			duration = -1
		}
		change_adm = 1
		change_dip = 1
		change_mil = 1
	}
}

on_estate_led_regency_surpassed = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			num_of_powerful_estates = 1
			has_estate_led_regency = {
				estate = any
			}
			NOT = {
				estate_led_regency_influence = 70
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_estate_led_regency = {
						estate = estate_burghers
					}
					NOT = {
						has_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
							estate = estate_church
							modifier = REFUSED_REGENCY
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
							estate = estate_nobles
							modifier = REFUSED_REGENCY
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_estate_led_regency = {
						estate = estate_church
					}
					NOT = {
						has_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
							estate = estate_burghers
							modifier = REFUSED_REGENCY
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
							estate = estate_nobles
							modifier = REFUSED_REGENCY
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_estate_led_regency = {
						estate = estate_nobles
					}
					NOT = {
						has_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
							estate = estate_burghers
							modifier = REFUSED_REGENCY
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						has_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
							estate = estate_church
							modifier = REFUSED_REGENCY
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = estate_regency_events.1 }
	}
}

##scope = colony province, FROM = owner country or province if there's a minority expulsion source, fires when the colony is created 1.35
on_colony_established = {
	if = {
		# Helper events since on_explore_coast and on_conquistador_empty don't fire without El Dorado
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_dlc = "El Dorado" }
			owner = { capital_scope = { continent = europe } }
			OR = {
				continent = north_america
				continent = south_america
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = new_world_discovered }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = castellar_mural_discovered }
			}
		}
		save_event_target_as = unraveling_colony
		owner = {
			country_event = { id = unraveling.90 }
			country_event = { id = unraveling.91 }
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_modifier = obrtrol_colonial_enthusiasm }
			OR = {
				superregion = gerudia_superregion
				region = northern_pass_region
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = obrtrol_troll_deal_accepted
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_nobles_tribes_tame_the_frontier_privilege }
			OR = {
				superregion = gerudia_superregion
				region = northern_pass_region
				region = yyl_moista_region
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = estate_tame_the_frontier_discount_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_modifier = vyzemby_colonial_fervour }
			province_group = amezatany_colonisation_provinces
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = vyzemby_amezatany_settlements
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = U08_cleared_coast }
			area = coastal_krahway_area
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = ekha_coastal_krahway_cleared
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = mb_all_the_world_reward_flg }
			OR = {
				area = orlghelovar_area
				area = south_altar_area
				area = north_altar_area
				area = argrod_origin_area
				province_id = 4093
				province_id = 2942
				province_id = 2943
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = mb_from_the_dark
			duration = 7300
		}
	}
	
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = A31_empire_colonial_office
					has_country_modifier = A31_traders_invest_economy
					has_country_modifier = A31_aiecoca_expanded
				}
				NOT = { has_country_modifier = elven_administration }
				NOT = {	has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration }

			}
			remove_country_modifier = A31_empire_colonial_office
			remove_country_modifier = A31_traders_invest_economy
			remove_country_modifier = A31_aiecoca_expanded
		}
	}
	if = { #Devandi Anglican Ability
		limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = seismic_sense_flag } }
		random_list = {
			55 = { change_trade_goods = copper }
			30 = { change_trade_goods = iron }
			15 = { change_trade_goods = gold }
		}
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = seismic_sense_flag }
	}

	if = { #Reveria Nostalgic Cold
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_country_flag = reveria_nostalgic_cold_flag }
			OR = {
				colonial_region = colonial_dalaire
				colonial_region = colonial_broken_sea
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = reveria_nostalgic_cold
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = { #Salla Elyn Moonlit Communities
			limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = I26_there_and_back_again_unlock }
			region = daravans_folly_region
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = I26_improved_moonlit_community_modifier }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = I26_improved_moonlit }
			}
			remove_province_modifier = I26_moonlit_community_modifier
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = I26_improved_moonlit_community_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = I26_moonlit_community_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	#Eighard
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_modifier = H14_to_the_north
			}
			ROOT = {
				has_any_winter_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_province_modifier = { #+25 settler growth, -20% colony cost
				name = H14_northern_expansion
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #Eighard
		limit = {
			has_climate = arctic
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					at_least_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 1 }
					overlord = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = H14_inner_warmth
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			continent = oceania
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_steel_tracking
					has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_steel_detector
				}
			}			
		}
		set_province_flag = precursor_steel_tracking
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				owns = 1016
				has_country_flag = sacred_grove_colonization_flag
			}
			1016 = { sacred_grove_usage_trigger = yes }
			region = bloodgroves_region
		}
		add_province_modifier = { name = sacred_grove_colonial_growth duration = -1 }
	}
}

#scope = new country, FROM = parent country 1.35
on_colonial_nation_established = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = no_aelantir_culture_switch }
			}
		}
		country_event = { 
			id = colonial_culture.2
			days = 18250
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_modifier = orcish_slaves_in_colonies
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = orcish_slaves_in_colonies
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				monstrous_culture = yes
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = monstrous.2 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = A01 } # Lorent 
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = A02 } # Deranne
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = A16 } # Wineport
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = A78 } # Roilsard
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = A09 } # Sorncost
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = A80 } # Iochand
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = H41 } # Sornicande
					has_country_flag = can_use_lencori_doctrine
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = can_use_lencori_doctrine
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					primary_culture = vernman
					primary_culture = valorman
					primary_culture = heartman
					has_country_flag = can_use_vernman_doctrine
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						tag = A55
						tag = A84
						tag = Z03
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = can_use_vernman_doctrine 
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			overlord = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = A33 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = can_get_half_ruinborn_pops_flag
	}
	if = { #For cleanup after venail annexation (deranne)
		limit = {
			overlord = { tag = A21 }
			A21 = { 
				overlord = { has_country_flag = deranne_integrate_venail_flag }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = deranne_integrate_venail_colony_flag
	}

	#Reveria
	if = { #Nostalgic Cold
		limit = {
			overlord = { 
				has_country_flag = reveria_nostalgic_cold_flag
			}
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					colonial_region = colonial_broken_sea
					colonial_region = colonial_dalaire
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = reveria_nostalgic_cold_flag
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			overlord = { 
				has_country_flag = reveria_ruined_sea_save
			}
			capital_scope = { colonial_region = colonial_isles }
		}
		override_country_name = REVERIARUINISLES
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = reveria_reaver_ruined_sea
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	#Zena
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { mission_completed = L06_deeper_into_effelai }
			capital_scope = {
				superregion = effelai_superregion
			}
		}
		change_religion = chahinanito
	}
}

on_institution_embracement = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_attribute = monarch_power_on_institutions
		}
		add_adm_power = 100
		add_dip_power = 100
		add_mil_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = {
				mission_completed = z22_prosperitys_champion
			}
			add_adm_power = 50
			add_dip_power = 50
			add_mil_power = 50
		}
	}
	if = { #Artificery start general
		limit = {
			has_institution = manufactories
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = artificery_unlocked
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { religion = bulwari_sun_cult }
				is_chosen_country = no
			}
		}
		if = { #corinsfield special event cause they dont like magick people
			limit = { tag = H35 }
			country_event = {
				id = flavour_corinsfield.79
			}
		}
		else_if = {# Gor Vazumbrog unlock full artificery
			limit = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = I14 }
			}
			country_event = { id = flavour_gor_vazumbrog.43 }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = anbennar_setup.19
			}
		}
	}
	if = { #Clearing the artificery cheese flag
		limit = { has_institution = manufactories }
		clr_country_flag = non_artificery_culture
	}
	if = { #Anbennar - isobelin events
		limit = {
			tag = G91
			has_institution = global_trade
		}
		country_event = { 
			id = flavor_isobelin.10 #goblin cartels
			days = 3650
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = G43 
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = haraf_has_reformed_kinah
			}
			2112 = {
                has_active_triggered_province_modifier = haraf_finished_integration
            }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = haraf_events.8
		}
		add_stability = -2
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = R03 } has_institution = manufactories }
		country_event = { id = sanghariyar.7 days = 3650 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { is_or_was_tag = { tag = R11 } has_institution = enlightenment }
		4532 = { remove_province_modifier = khadisrapur_early_coal_power }
	}
	if = { #Anzalkatsa School Fight Embrace Events
		limit = { 
			religion = anzalkatsa
			NOT = { has_global_flag = 333rdformed } 
		}
	
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_institution = renaissance
				NOT = { has_global_flag = LizardEmbracedRenaissance }
			}
			anb_lizardfolk_clash_change_variable_minus = yes
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				country_event = { id = AnzalkatsaSchoolFightEvents.4 }
			}
			set_global_flag = LizardEmbracedRenaissance
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_institution = new_world_i
				NOT = { has_global_flag = LizardEmbracedColonialism }
			}
			anb_lizardfolk_clash_change_variable_minus = yes
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				country_event = { id = AnzalkatsaSchoolFightEvents.5 }
			}
			set_global_flag = LizardEmbracedColonialism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_institution = printing_press
				NOT = { has_global_flag = LizardEmbracedPrint }
			}
			anb_lizardfolk_clash_change_variable_plus = yes
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				country_event = { id = AnzalkatsaSchoolFightEvents.6 }
			}
			set_global_flag = LizardEmbracedPrint
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_institution = global_trade
				NOT = { has_global_flag = LizardEmbracedGlobalTrade }
			}
			anb_lizardfolk_clash_change_variable_plus = yes
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					religion = anzalkatsa
				}
				country_event = { id = AnzalkatsaSchoolFightEvents.7 }
			}
			set_global_flag = LizardEmbracedGlobalTrade
		}
	}

	#Pashaine
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = B59 } 
			has_institution = manufactories
			adm_tech = 21
			303 = { has_province_flag = change_to_coal } 
		}
		303 = { change_trade_goods = coal }
	}

	accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = sponsor_travelling_libraries category = adm amount = 100 }

	# karakhanbar upgrade smelters
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = Z54 } 
			has_institution = manufactories
			has_country_modifier = karakhanbar_prototype_smelters
		}
		country_event = { id = flavour_karakhanbar.14 }
	}
}

#ROOT = new capital province, FROM = old capital province
on_capital_moved = {
	on_capital_moved_effect = yes
	# if your capital is moved to a colony (i.e. by losing all your other provinces)
	# this colony auto-completes to a province without triggering on_colony_finished
	# so catch this edge case here to fix the pop modifiers
	# stupidly, when it triggers this on_action it's both a colony and your capital
	if = {
		limit = { is_colony = yes }
		province_event = { id = race_setup_events.15 }
	}

	# to avoid an emperor in the new world (specifically during the league wars, where the leagues then become unjoinable)
	# added by anbennar since EoA members commonly colonise
	if = {
		limit = {
		 	owner = { is_emperor = yes  }
			NOT = { owner = { capital_scope = { continent = europe }}}
			NOT = { # once peace is guaranteed, this trigger is superfluous
				hre_reform_passed = anbennar_mages_peace
				hre_reform_passed = anbennar_empower_imperial_diet
			}
		}
		owner = { set_emperor = no }
	}


	if = { limit = { has_province_modifier = cant_colonize }	#Anbennar
		province_event = { id = migration_force_settle.3 days = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		if = { #Extra dev cost reduction in capital for being the Sri Baginda
			limit = {
				owner = { is_sri_baginda = yes }
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = sri_baginda_lower_dev_cost_capital_mod }
			}
			FROM = {
				area = {
					remove_province_modifier = sri_baginda_lower_dev_cost_capital_mod
				}
			}
			area = {
				limit = { owner = { is_sri_baginda = yes } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = sri_baginda_lower_dev_cost_capital_mod
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #removes/sets dev cost bonus on capital state for government reforms
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_government_attribute = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state_modifier }
			}
			FROM = {
				area = {
					limit = { owner = { owns = ROOT } }
					remove_province_modifier = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state_modifier
				}
			}
			area = {
				limit = { owner = { owns = ROOT } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = lower_dev_cost_in_capital_state_modifier
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	
		#Anbennar
		if = { #removes/sets gov cost bonus on capital region for government reforms
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_government_attribute = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region
				}
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region_modifier }
			}
			FROM = {
				region = {
					limit = { owner = { owns = ROOT } }
					remove_province_modifier = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region_modifier
				}
			}
			region = {
				limit = { owner = { owns = ROOT } }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = lower_gov_cost_in_home_region_modifier
					duration = -1
					hidden = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	owner = {	
		country_event = { id = escanni_wars.3 } # Escanni wars bypass
		country_event = { id = escanni_wars.200 } # Joined Escanni wars
		country_event = { id = flavour_splinter.2 } # Itinerant Capital
	}
	
	#update "Religion Triumphant" HRE modifiers
	owner = { country_event = { id = religious_leagues.11 } }
	
	#dwarovar reclaimer
	if = { limit = { continent = serpentspine }
		owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = reclaiming_dwarovar duration = -1 } }
	}
	else = {
		owner = { remove_country_modifier = reclaiming_dwarovar }
	}

	FROM = { #Close hold digging gui on old capital
		clr_province_flag = diggy_diggy_estimate_flag
	}

	# move "arcane battery capital complex" invention
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_arcane_battery_capital_complex
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_province_modifier = artifice_arcane_battery_capital_complex
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_arcane_battery_capital_complex
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	
	yrw_move_iosahar_debug_modifier = yes

	sedentarization_on_capital_moved = yes

	#CENTAUR NOMADISM
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government_attribute = centaur_nomadism_attribute
			}
			add_nomadic_capital_moved_modifier = { scope = ROOT }
			apply_owned_NZOC_country = yes
			if = {
				limit = { ai = no }
				country_event = { id = centaur_nomad.1 days = 1096 } #3 years
				update_nomadism_capital_move_cost = yes
				if = {
					limit = { #Black Herd
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								has_province_modifier = I55_tomb_of_the_unchained
								has_province_modifier = I55_home_of_the_greatbound
								has_province_modifier = I55_land_of_the_frostclaimed
							}
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = centaur_nomad.1 days = 366 } } #1 year
				}
			}
		}
	}
	#Bonecarver
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_country_flag = B27_wwc }
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = B27_werewolf_convocation }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = B27_werewolf_convocation
			duration = -1
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_province_modifier = B27_werewolf_convocation
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_country_flag = B27_corpse_of_dookan_holder }
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = B27_corpse_of_dookanson }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = B27_corpse_of_dookanson
			duration = -1
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_province_modifier = B27_corpse_of_dookanson
		}
	}
	#Irkorzik itinerant capital
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_reform = irkorzik_dunesworn_council_reform } }
		ROOT = {
			owner = {
				capital_scope = { set_province_flag = F69_capital_counter }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = irkorzik_capital_moved
					duration = 1825
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = irkorzik_itinerant_capital } }
			ROOT = {
				owner = {
					every_owned_province = {
						limit = { has_province_modifier = irkorzik_capital }
						remove_province_modifier = irkorzik_capital
					}
					capital_scope = { 
						every_province_in_state = { 
							add_permanent_province_modifier = {
								name = irkorzik_capital
								duration = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = irkorzik_itinerant_capital_bonus_church_power } }
			ROOT = {
				owner = {
					add_church_power = 40
				}
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { is_part_of_hre = yes }
			hre_reform_passed = anbennar_internal_divisions
		}
		ROOT = {
			owner = {
				refresh_court_bonus = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#karassk itinerant capital
	if = {
		limit = { 
			owner = {
				has_reform = karassk_laushan_city
			}
			has_port = yes 
		}
		owner = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = L68_capital_sail_cooldown 
				duration = 1825 
			}
			capital_scope = {
				every_province_in_state = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = L68_the_black_and_red_sails_of_blood_duty
						duration = 1825
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				province_id = 5898
			}
			remove_province_modifier = L68_the_first_seat
		}
		else = {
			5898 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = L68_the_first_seat
					duration = -1 
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_flag = L68_move_with_cap
				}
			}
			owner = {
				capital_scope = {
					every_province_in_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_province_modifier = L68_merfolk_slaves
							}
						}
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = L68_merfolk_slaves
							duration = 1825
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									ROOT = {
										6009 = {
											has_great_project = {
												type = arskitse_evil_karassk
												tier = 2
											}
										}
									}
								}
								add_province_modifier = {
									name = L68_emperors_of_arskite
									duration = 1825
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# On occasion, released nations will attempt to move capital to a province they don't own
	# This causes issues because now ROOT can get additional copies of magical fortress
	# However, we also need to account for cases where capitals get annexed (FROM owned by conquerer)
	# Therefore, the best solution is to just check if the new province is actually a capital
	# This problem was uncovered by @caudex on Discord and solved by @bonbonny01 (me)
	# Technically, the problem persists if tag A attempts to move to the capital of tag B, and they both have levels of this project.

	if = {
		limit = { is_capital = yes } #Check if ROOT is actually a capital, reduces edge cases
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = magical_fortress level = 3 } } }
			FROM = {
				remove_province_modifier = magical_fortress_mod_3
				remove_province_modifier = abjuration_1_ward_mod_3
				hidden_effect = { province_event = { id = kheionai.2 } }
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = magical_fortress_mod_3 duration = -1 }
			add_province_modifier = { name = abjuration_1_ward_mod_3 duration = -1 }
			hidden_effect = { province_event = { id = kheionai.2 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = magical_fortress level = 2 } } }
			FROM = {
				remove_province_modifier = magical_fortress_mod_2
				remove_province_modifier = abjuration_1_ward_mod_2
				hidden_effect = { province_event = { id = kheionai.2 } }
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = magical_fortress_mod_2 duration = -1 }
			add_province_modifier = { name = abjuration_1_ward_mod_2 duration = -1 }
			hidden_effect = { province_event = { id = kheionai.2 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { owner = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = magical_fortress level = 1 } } }
			FROM = {
				remove_province_modifier = magical_fortress_mod_1
				remove_province_modifier = abjuration_1_ward_mod_1
			}
			add_province_modifier = { name = magical_fortress_mod_1 duration = -1 }
			add_province_modifier = { name = abjuration_1_ward_mod_1 duration = -1 }
		}
	}

	FROM = {
		if = { #Black Herd
			limit = { has_province_modifier = I55_home_of_the_greatbound_sub }
			remove_province_modifier = I55_home_of_the_greatbound_sub
		}
	}

	#Lupulan rangers
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_reform = yanglam_tengalam_reform
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_province_modifier = lupulan_base_rangers_modifier
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = lupulan_base_rangers_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				owner = {
					is_sri_baginda = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = tier_1_baginda
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				remove_province_modifier = sri_baginda_rangers_1
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = sri_baginda_rangers_1
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					owner = {
						has_country_flag = tier_2_baginda
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				remove_province_modifier = sri_baginda_rangers_2
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = sri_baginda_rangers_2
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				remove_province_modifier = sri_baginda_rangers_3
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = sri_baginda_rangers_3
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_reform = pelimkana_kalemba_reform
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_province_modifier = pelimkana_base_rangers_modifier
		}
		ROOT = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = pelimkana_base_rangers_modifier
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#ROOT = province that was expanded in, FROM = country that did it
on_expanded_infrastructure = {
	events = {
		flavour_gor_vazumbrog.209
	}
	# Ovdal Tungr Uthojdihr Trading Post system.
	F23_apply_uthojdihr_trading_post = yes
	
	if = { #Stalbor
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				AND = {
					has_reform = book_of_stone
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = arturo_meny_open
					}
				}
			}
			has_province_modifier = arturos_watch_chapter
		}
		province_event = { id = flavor_stalbor.2 }
	}

	if = { #Ikogshaantus
		limit = { 
			has_province_modifier = J52_consecrated_industry 
			FROM = { has_reform = ikogshaantus_khantaar_industrial_council }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = J52_industrial_rush
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = rightful_xia_territory
			FROM = {
				tag = Y89
				has_country_flag = xia_has_territory_buff
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = yuanszi_specialized }
		}
		yuanszi_assign_specialization = yes
	}

	#Pashaine
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = expand_infrastructure_goods_rep_zeal  } }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = pashaine_economic_boom
			duration = 1825 #5 years
		}
		owner = {
			add_republican_tradition = 1
			add_revolutionary_zeal = 1
		}
	}

	if = { #Kheionai Gov Reforms
		limit = { 
			FROM = { has_reform = kheionai_the_urban_litea } 
			OR = {
				has_terrain = city_terrain
				has_province_modifier = kheionai_the_urban_litea_prov_mod
			}
		}
		add_urban_litea_modifiers = yes
	}

	# Bibyobi
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = S98_supplanting_tamajoba_finished
			}
			has_province_modifier = ironwood_trees
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = S98_ironwood_improved
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_reform = warehouse_of_gerudia_doctrine }
			superregion = gerudia_superregion
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = expand_infrastructure_cost_modifier 
						value = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { add_adm_power = 25 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_global_modifier_value = {
						which = expand_infrastructure_cost_modifier 
						value = 0.8
					}
				}
			}
			owner = { add_adm_power = 10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_1
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_2
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_2
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_3
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_3
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_4
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_4
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_5
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_5 }
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_1
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	#Molten Eternity
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = speaking_memory_responsibility
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = 250
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_bureau }
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = artifice_invention_mech_bureau_mod }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
				name = artifice_invention_mech_bureau_mod
				duration = -1
		}
	}

	if = { #Orenvalyam
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = U39_kavalalist_parliament_buff_flag } }
		owner = { change_government_reform_progress = 25 }
		add_local_autonomy = -15
	}

	if = {
		limit = { #Karach
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = karach_Expand_Infrastructure_Canvas
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = karach_expand_infra }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = karach_expand_infra
			duration = -1
		}
		karach_Workshops = yes
		FROM = {
			ashhana_blood_curse_add_control_by_source = {
				canvas_strength = 2
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_terrain_shaper }
		}
		add_province_triggered_modifier = ptm_add_random_dev
	}

	if = { #Sacred Grove rank 2
		limit = {
			1016 = {
				owned_by = FROM
				has_great_project = { type = sacred_grove tier = 2 }
				sacred_grove_usage_trigger = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = sacred_grove_infra_offset }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = sacred_grove_infra_offset
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

on_expanded_infrastructure_removed = {
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = expand_infrastructure_goods_rep_zeal  } }
		remove_province_modifier = pashaine_economic_boom
        owner = {
			add_republican_tradition = -1
			add_revolutionary_zeal = -1	
		}
	}

	if = { #Kheionai Gov Reforms
		limit = { 
			FROM = { has_reform = kheionai_the_urban_litea } 
			has_province_modifier = kheionai_the_urban_litea_prov_mod
		}
		add_urban_litea_modifiers = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_reform = warehouse_of_gerudia_doctrine } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_1
			}
			remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_2
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_1
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_3
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_2
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_4
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_3
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_5
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_4
				duration = -1
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_province_modifier = warehouse_of_gerudia_mod_5
			}
		}
	}
	#Molten Eternity
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = speaking_memory_responsibility
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = -250
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_mech_bureau }
			NOT = { num_of_times_expanded_infrastructure = 1 }
		}
		remove_province_modifier = artifice_invention_mech_bureau_mod
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_terrain_shaper }
		}
		remove_random_development = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = sacred_grove_infra_offset
			NOT = { num_of_times_expanded_infrastructure = 1 }
		}
		remove_province_modifier = sacred_grove_infra_offset
	}
}

#ROOT = province that was centralized in
on_centralized_state = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_government_attribute = centralize_state_no_reform_cost }
		}
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = 50
			change_government_reform_progress = 50
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_government_attribute = centralize_state_half_refund NOT = { has_age_ability = ab_ruinborn_empire } }
		}
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = 25
			change_government_reform_progress = 25
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { 
				OR = {
					has_government_attribute = centralize_state_development
					has_age_ability = ab_ruinborn_empire
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			limit = {
				owned_by = ROOT
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
				1 = { add_base_production = 1 }
				1 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				religion = drozma_tur
				has_church_aspect = aspire_wisdom_aspect_adm
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_church_power = 10
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_country_flag = centralize_state_half_refund_random_dev
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
			1 = { add_base_production = 1 }
			1 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
		}
		owner = {
			add_adm_power = 25
			change_government_reform_progress = 25
		}
	}
	#Ibekisedara
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				province_id = 5554 #Weriksedar
				province_id = 6638 #Dochiberra
				province_id = 6665 #Adebakore
			}
			owner = { tag = S61 }
		}
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = S61_centralized_werikafan_flag
		}	
	}
	#Dragon Turtle
	owner = { dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = naauao amount = 15 } }
}

on_hre_dismantled = {
	#updates "Religion Triumphant" HRE modifiers
	hidden_effect = { every_country = { country_event = { id = religious_leagues.11 } } }
	country_event = { id = hre_event.15 }
	if = { 
		limit = { has_country_flag = A49_dismantling_hre }
		country_event = { id = flavour_xanzerbexis.19 } #Fallen Empire
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = { remove_court_bonus = yes }
		every_province = { remove_province_modifier = eoa_occupied_temple }
	}
}

#ROOT = province
on_adm_exploited = {
	anb_on_exploit_effect = { dev = tax }
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = may_not_reduce_tax_on_exploitation } }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_base_tax = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = may_not_reduce_tax_on_own_exploitation culture_group = ROOT } }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			add_base_tax = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_government_attribute = may_not_reduce_tax_on_foreign_exploitation NOT = { culture_group = ROOT } } }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_base_tax = 1
		}
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					religion = summer_court
					religion = winter_court
				}				
			}
		}
		owner = { add_church_power = -4 }
	}
	#Salla Ayeth MT
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = I33_forest_to_be_cut
		}
		clr_province_flag = I33_forest_to_be_cut
	}
	#Ibekisedara
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { tag = S61 }
			OR = {
				province_id = 5564
				province_id = 5566
				province_id = 5578
			}
		}
		set_province_flag = S61_exploited_adm_dev_flag
	}
	if = { #Dbco
		limit = {
			owner = {
				tag = S30
			}
		}
		set_province_flag = S30_exploit
	}
	#Eighard
	if = {
		limit = {
			1990 = {
				has_province_modifier = H14_salting_the_fields
			}
			owner = {
				tag = H14
				owns_or_non_sovereign_subject_of = 1990 #Raithtall
			}
		}
		trigger_switch = { #Exploiting Tax Dev gives +10 gold per level of base tax in province post-exploit, up to a max of 100 crowns
			on_trigger = base_tax

			10 = { owner = { add_treasury = 100 } }
			9 = { owner = { add_treasury = 90 } }
			8 = { owner = { add_treasury = 80 } }
			7 = { owner = { add_treasury = 70 } }
			6 = { owner = { add_treasury = 60 } }
			5 = { owner = { add_treasury = 50 } }
			4 = { owner = { add_treasury = 40 } }
			3 = { owner = { add_treasury = 30 } }
			2 = { owner = { add_treasury = 20 } }
			1 = { owner = { add_treasury = 10 } }
		}
	}
}
