on_raze = {
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = anb_on_action_tracking_raze_flag } }
		set_province_flag = anb_has_been_razed_flag
	}
	add_permanent_province_modifier = {
		name = province_razed
		duration = 7300
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = xhazobkult_ritualized_cleansing has_estate_privilege = xhazobkult_ritualized_cleansing_clergy } } }
		xhazobkult_terrain_razing = yes
	}
	owner = {
		change_variable = {
			which = nbProvincesRazed
			value = 1
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = nbProvincesRazedByRuler
			value = 1
		}
	}
	owner = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = rakkaz_gain_more_demonic_power }
			add_patriarch_authority = 0.005
		}
		if = {
			limit = { religion = kvangahga }
			add_church_power = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = unlocked_reaver_personality_flag
				NOT = { ruler_has_personality = reaver_personality }
				check_variable = {
					which = nbProvincesRazedByRuler
					value = 30
				}
			}
			force_add_ruler_personality = { personality = reaver_personality }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_government_attribute = scourge_of_irdaeos_reform_raze_effect }
			has_base_nomadic_zone_of_control_modifier = yes
		}
		export_to_variable = {
    		which = scourgeDev
    		value = development
    		who = ROOT
		}
		while = {
            limit = {
                #While our total dip value has 1, lower dip power by 1.
                check_variable = {
                    which = scourgeDev
                    value = 1
                }
            }
            owner = {
				add_treasury = 5
			}
            subtract_variable = {
                which = scourgeDev
                value = 1
            }
        }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = rakkaz_church_power_on_raze } }
		owner = { add_church_power = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_country_flag = rakkaz_more_devastation } }
		add_devastation = 10
	}
	owner = { #Saqraxat
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = L04_let_slip_the_hounds }
			extend_country_modifier = {
				name = L04_let_slip_the_hounds
				duration = 365
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				is_or_was_tag = { tag = L76 }
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = L76_pain_into_weapons_1
					has_country_modifier = L76_pain_into_weapons_2
				}
			}
		}
		owner = { L76_razing_effect = yes }
	}

}

on_concentrate_development = {
	if = { #1.35
		limit = { 
			owner = { has_country_modifier = fra_french_isles_modifier }
		}
		add_nationalism = -5
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = S90
					tag = S30
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = S90_concentrate
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# EVERYTHING BELOW 1.35
on_slacken_start = {
    if = { #no slacken pls
        limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = no_slacken_mod
				has_country_modifier = spirit_military
			}
        }
        add_army_professionalism = 0.01
    }
    else = {
        add_country_modifier = {
            name = slackening_modifier
            duration = -1
        }
    }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				was_tag = A95
				tag = A95
			}
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = sailors_when_slacken
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = sailors_when_slacken duration = -1 }
	}
}
on_slacken_stop = {
	remove_country_modifier = slackening_modifier
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				was_tag = A95
				tag = A95
			}
			ai = no
			has_country_flag = sailors_when_slacken
		}
		remove_country_modifier = sailors_when_slacken
	}
}

on_colony_finished = { #ROOT - Province
	events = {
		kheionai.99 #Fires the nekhei province transfer effects so the game doesn't crash
		gerudia.35 #Taric and Cagodic stuff
		flavour_zokka.9998 #zokka slave state limit to spine
	}
	on_colony_finished_effect = yes

	# Anbennar
	province_event = { id = race_setup_events.15 }	
	# colonies do not get their pops updated to match the owners (even though the culture is the owners primary)
	# until the colony is complete

	g27_breluslad_supplies_effect = yes
	g27_breluslad_village_elections_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_monstrous_tribes_promise_new_lands } }
		owner = { change_estate_land_share = { estate = estate_monstrous_tribes share = 1 } }
	}

	#Beggaston
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_country_modifier = beggaston_sarda_pioneers
			}
			region = veykoda_region
		}
		change_culture = sarda
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = U08_cleared_coast }
			area = coastal_krahway_area
		}
		ROOT = {
		remove_province_modifier = ekha_coastal_krahway_cleared
		}
	}
	#Half-Elves

on_advisor_hired = { #ROOT - Country
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = S50_shadow_pact_fortune_tellers
				has_country_flag = S50_pack_leaders
				has_country_flag = S50_sharp_tongues
				has_country_flag = S50_diplomatic_liasons
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = yemotaferi.13 days = 1 } # Hidden event to update advisor modifiers
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			dragon_turtle_hated_or_below = { dragon_turtle = makaoioi }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = makaoioi_double_up }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25
			set_country_flag = makaoioi_double_up
			country_event = { id = dragon_turtles.122 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

on_adm_advisor_hired = { #ROOT - Country, executed after on_advisor_hired!
	#Pasiragha phlisosopher mods based on scholar invited #WHY IS THIS FIRING AN EVENT YOU MIGHT ASK??? #HAHAHAHAHAHAHA
	#turns out this fires before you have technically employed the new advisor, so you can't check if you hired a specific advisor type 
	if = { limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = pasiragha_flag_improved_philosophers } } ROOT = { country_event = { id = flavor_pasiragha.3 days = 1 } } }
	
	set_country_flag = adm_advisor_recently_hired
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = accretive_path
			OR = {
				has_church_aspect = accretive_path_acts_of_hermitage_unimproved
				has_church_aspect = accretive_path_acts_of_hermitage_improved
			}
		}
		add_church_power = 25
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { accretive_path_adm_chi = 25 } }
	}

	#Ashhana Lizardfolk gain Canvas Control for advisors
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_government_mechanic = ashhana_blood_curse_mechanic
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = ashhana_control_adm_advisor
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}

	# Parusahan Saya MT - Right-Hand Mage check
	if = {
		limit = { 
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = R54 }
			mission_completed = R54_bow_mage_and_fall 
			employed_advisor = { type = court_mage }
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = R54_right_hand_mage duration = -1 }
	}
}

on_core = { #ROOT - Province, #FROM - Country that gets the core
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { OR = { religion = gods_of_the_taychend religion = oren_nayiru } } }
		FROM = { gain_taychend_glory_effect = { amount = 10 } }
	}
	#Restoring upgrades if an order was deactivated but not destroyed due to the state only being partially conquered (and you losing the core in the meantime)
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_balgar }
			holy_order = balgar_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_balgar_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_corin }
			holy_order = corin_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_corin_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			owner = { has_country_flag = upgraded_falah }
			holy_order = falah_order
			area_for_scope_province  = {
				type = all
				owner = {
					ROOT = { owned_by = PREV }
					is_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		area = {
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = corinite_falah_upgraded
				duration = -1
			}
		}

	else_if = {

				type = all

	else_if = {

	#naleni rebels
	if = {

			limit = {

			} #beri gnidi

	}
}

on_tech_taken = { #ROOT - Country
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = spring_court
		}
		add_church_power = 50
	}

	#Drozma Tur
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = drozma_tur
			has_church_aspect = aspire_wisdom_aspect_dip
		}
		add_church_power = 20
		change_government_reform_progress = 10
	}
	accretive_path_gain_chi = { aspect = words_aflame category = adm amount = 50 }

	if = { #Magic Rework
		limit = { has_country_modifier = orb_of_omniscience_tech_tracker }
		change_variable = { orb_of_omniscience_progress_tracker = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = V05_stewards_of_past_flag }
		set_variable = {
			which = count_conjuration_spell_mana 
			value = 0
		}
		remove_country_modifier = V05_stewards_of_past_1
		remove_country_modifier = V05_stewards_of_past_2
		remove_country_modifier = V05_stewards_of_past_3
		remove_country_modifier = V05_stewards_of_past_4
		remove_country_modifier = V05_stewards_of_past_5
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = V05_stewards_of_past_0
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = { tag_allowed_dragon_turtle_system = yes }
		dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = vea amount = 6 }
		dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = grandfather_moss amount = 6 }
		dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = kahuzaie amount = 6 }
	}
	if = {

		}

}

on_barrage = { #ROOT - barraging country, FROM - barraged province
	if = {	#set the country flag to begin counting
		limit = { has_country_flag = count_barrages_done }
		change_variable = {
			which = artilleryBarrageUsed
			value = 1
		}
	}
	overlord = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = count_barrages_done }
			change_variable = {
				which = artilleryBarrageUsed
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = {
				tag = S81 #Khatalashya
				has_country_modifier = khatalashya_butterflies
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = khatalashya_butterflies_province
				duration = 365
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_cast_elemental_fury = yes
				has_cast_flaming_munitions = yes
			}
			FROM = {
				province_not_immune_to_siege_magic = yes
				NOT = { has_province_modifier = fireball_cheese_protection }
			}
		}
		FROM = { ROOT = { evocation_0_fireball_effect = yes } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_scream_beamers }
		if = {
			limit = { mission_completed = F98_elemental_artifice }
			FROM = { change_siege = 3 }
		}
		else = { FROM = { change_siege = 2 } }
	}

	if = { #Orenvalyam
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = U39_vaikaranayiru_flag
			has_cast_elemental_fury = yes
			has_mana = { amount = 25 }
		}
		change_mana = { amount = -25 }
		FROM = { ROOT = { evocation_2_meteor_swarm_effect = yes } } #So the PREV in the effect targets the province
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_estate_privilege = artifice_invention_seed_siege
		}
		FROM = {
			add_devastation = 50
			if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 10
				}
				add_garrison = -2000
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 9
				}
				add_garrison = -1800
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 8
				}
				add_garrison = -1600
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 7
				}
				add_garrison = -1400
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 6
				}
				add_garrison = -1200
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 5
				}
				add_garrison = -1000
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 4
				}
				add_garrison = -800
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 3
				}
				add_garrison = -600
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fort_level = 2
				}
				add_garrison = -400
			}
			else = {
				add_garrison = -200
			}
		}
	}
}

on_naval_barrage = { #ROOT - barraging country, FROM - barraged province
	if = {
		limit = {

				has_cast_elemental_fury = yes
				has_cast_flaming_munitions = yes
			}
			FROM = {

				NOT = { has_province_modifier = fireball_cheese_protection }
			}
		}
		FROM = { ROOT = { evocation_0_fireball_effect = yes } }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_naval_doctrine = bulwar_kamelyan_tactics }
		FROM = { change_siege = 3 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_modifier = RSP_trollshaunt_krakens_kiss_prepared }
		remove_country_modifier = RSP_trollshaunt_krakens_kiss_prepared
		FROM = { 
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = RSP_trollshaunt_dreaded_mist
				duration = 1095
			}
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			927 = {
				country_or_subject_holds = ROOT
				has_great_project = { type = column_of_alariandel tier = 2 }
				can_owner_use_colonial_monuments = yes
				has_fort_building_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = { change_siege = 1 }
	}
}

on_scorch_earth = { #ROOT - scorching country, FROM - scorched province
	FROM = {
		on_scorch_earth_effect = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			ROOT = { 
				has_country_flag = karakhanbar_powerful_scorch_earth
				has_wartaxes = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				limit = {
					controlled_by = ROOT
					NOT = { has_province_modifier = scorched_earth }
				}
				add_devastation = 10
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = scorched_earth
					duration = 1825
				}
				on_scorch_earth_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			is_or_was_tag = { tag = Y17 } #Gushuokguan
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = gushuokguan_scorched_earth_counter
			value = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = J78
			has_country_flag = rat_kings_alive
		}
		FROM = { set_province_flag = uesrennu_people_to_arms }
		add_or_extend_country_modifier = {
			name = uesrennu_sated_swarm
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 5 limit = "capital_scope = { superregion = taychend_superregion }" }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = uesrennu_scorched } }
			FROM = { save_event_target_as = uesrennu_scorched_province }
			country_event = { id = uesrennu.2 }
		}
	}
}

			has_personal_deity = speaking_memory_tradition
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moltenEternityObligationVar
			value = -150
		}
	}
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = speaking_memory_tradition
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = -150
			}
		}
	}
	FROM = { dragon_turtle_change_friendship = { dragon_turtle = makaoioi amount = -5 } }
}

on_alliance_created = { #ROOT - Alliance sender, FROM - Alliance accepter
	If = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = A75_alenic_blood_flag
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = A75_alenic_blood
			}
			FROM = {
				tag = A30
			}
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = A75_alenic_blood
			duration = -1
			desc = UNTIL_ALLIANCE_BROKEN
		}
		FROM = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = A75_alenic_blood
				duration = -1
				desc = UNTIL_ALLIANCE_BROKEN
			}
		}
	}
}

on_royal_marriage = { #ROOT - Marraige sender, FROM - marriage accepter
	#Molten Eternity
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = molten_eternity
			has_personal_deity = speaking_memory_tradition
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = moltenEternityObligationVar
			value = 150
		}
	}
	FROM = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = molten_eternity
				has_personal_deity = speaking_memory_tradition
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = moltenEternityObligationVar
				value = 150
			}
		}
	}
}

on_heir_disinherited = {
	magic_on_heir_death = yes
	if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_mongoose_shifter
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_leopard_shifter
				has_country_modifier = heir_is_elephant_shifter
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = heir_is_mongoose_shifter
        remove_country_modifier = heir_is_leopard_shifter
        remove_country_modifier = heir_is_elephant_shifter
	}

	if = { #Caergaraen
		limit = { has_country_modifier = J74_saerasyar_sword_base_mod }
		country_event = {
			id = caergaraen.2 #Judging The Guilty
		}
	}
}		
on_overrun = { #ROOT - winner, FROM - loser, on stackwipe
	if = { #Black Herd
		limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_mages_black_herd_shockshroud_mages }
		change_mana = { amount = 1.5 }
	}
	if = { #Gasha
		limit = { has_country_modifier = L76_khagaarsa }
		if = { 
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { has_country_flag = khagaarsa_explained } } }
			FROM = { country_event = { id = flavour_gasha.10 } }
		}
		else = {
			FROM = { add_country_modifier = { name = L76_terrified_by_khagaarsa duration = 365 } }
		}
	}
}
